# 10 — Kiến trúc & luồng hoạt động (as-built)

> Tài liệu **bám sát code thực tế** (khác với `00`–`09` là design-intent). Mọi mô tả ở đây đối chiếu
> với mã nguồn hiện hành, link tới `file:line` thật. Nếu code đổi, cập nhật lại file này.
>
> **Lưu ý lệch so với design docs:** một số điểm trong `00`/`04` đã không còn khớp hiện thực — xem mục
> [Khác biệt so với design docs](#khác-biệt-so-với-design-docs) ở cuối.

## 1. Bản chất

VPN client **thuần userspace**: tự cài đặt toàn bộ ngăn xếp (IKE, ESP, L2TP, PPP, SSTP, TCP/IP) ở tầng
ứng dụng, **không cần TUN/TAP adapter của OS, không ghi bảng route hệ thống**. Ứng dụng nhận một IP ảo
trong đường hầm rồi mở TCP/UDP socket chạy *bên trong* đường hầm.

Hai triết lý:
- **Plugin theo driver** — mỗi giao thức là một `IVpnProtocolDriver`, đăng ký theo tên (`"sstp"`, `"l2tp-ipsec"`, `"ikev2"`).
- **Đảo ngược phụ thuộc** — mọi tầng chỉ phụ thuộc project `Abstractions`, không phụ thuộc ngang.

## 2. Phân lớp (24 project trong `src/`)

```
APP       TqkLibrary.VpnClient            VpnClient / VpnClientBuilder   (entry point)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Sockets   VpnTcpClient / VpnUdpClient / VpnNetworkStream
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
DRIVER    TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.L2tpIpsec   (IKEv1 + ESP + L2TP + PPP — lắp ráp toàn bộ stack; ESP-in-UDP/4500 NAT-T mặc định, hoặc native ESP proto-50 qua Transport.RawIp khi HonestFirst + no-NAT — P0.8c)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp        (TLS + PPP + crypto binding — refs Abstractions+Ppp)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ikev2       (IKEv2 + ESP tunnel mode — không PPP; V.1)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn     (OpenVPN tun: UDP/TCP + TLS-in-control + AEAD — không PPP; V2.h)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.WireGuard   (WireGuard: UDP + Noise_IKpsk2 + data type-4 + config tĩnh — không PPP; V3.f)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther   (SoftEther SSL-VPN: TLS + Ethernet-over-TLS + DHCP/ARP/VirtualHost bridge 1-host hoac multi-host broadcast domain opt-in (uplink-as-port) — driver L2 that; V4.c; multi-connection 1-32 socket/1 session qua SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux — V.4; IPv6 trong tunnel opt-in enableIpv6: NDISC v6 (L2.4) + SLAAC/DHCPv6 (L2.6) qua DualStack* (L2.9) best-effort tren bridge SecureNAT — V.4-ipv6)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect (OpenConnect/ocserv: TLS byte-stream + HTTPS config-auth + HTTP CONNECT + CSTP data plane + DPD/keepalive + rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-* (re-establish make-before-break) — không PPP; data plane qua DTLS 1.2 khi server đẩy X-DTLS-* (Transport.Dtls/F.3), fallback CSTP-over-TLS; V5.b/V5.c/V5.d)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core        (scaffolding dùng chung: ReconnectingVpnConnection<TState> supervisor + VpnReconnectOptions — gom EstablishAsync/ReconnectLoopAsync/backoff-jitter/StateChanged/link-loss; consumer WireGuard + OpenConnect + OpenVPN + SoftEther + SSTP + IKEv2 + L2TP/IPsec — F.6 xong cho mọi driver)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp        (PPTP RFC 2637: control TCP/1723 + GRE proto-47 qua IRawIpTransportFactory + MPPE + PPP/MS-CHAPv2 — Echo keepalive, auto-reconnect F.6; legacy/insecure; OFFLINE code+test, live chờ Q.1; V6.b)
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
PROTOCOL  TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec     Ike/V1 , Ike/V2 , Esp , Nat (NAT-T UDP 500↔4500, ghép kênh IKE/ESP)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp      L2TPv2 control + data
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp       LCP / IPCP / IPV6CP / MS-CHAPv2 / HDLC + Ipv6/ (global IPv6 over PPP: RS/RA/SLAAC/DHCPv6 qua PppEthernetChannelAdapter tái dùng engine Ethernet NDISC/SLAAC — P1.1; refs Ethernet)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack   IPv4+IPv6 / TCP / UDP / ICMP userspace (dual-stack)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet  L2 Ethernet: codec frame/MAC + EthernetSwitch hoc MAC (host-port + uplink-port ConnectUplink) + VirtualHost bridge + ARP IPv4 + NDISC IPv6 + DHCPv4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6 client + EthernetAdapter rap multi-host + MultiHostSession (N station = N IVpnSession) + composite dual-stack (DualStackNeighborResolver/Configurator) (L2.0-L2.9)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn   OpenVPN: codec + reliability + TLS-in-control + tls-auth/crypt + data channel (AEAD GCM/ChaCha + non-AEAD AES-CBC+HMAC qua IOpenVpnDataChannel) + P_DATA_V1/V2 + push/keepalive + NCP + TCP/UDP/tap (V.2, tun-UDP validate live VPN Gate)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard WireGuard: handshake Noise_IKpsk2 + codec type-1/2/3 + TAI64N + mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply + data channel type-4 (counter u64 + anti-replay 64-gói + keepalive) + timers/state machine rekey/keepalive + WireGuardConfig/WireGuardPeer/WireGuardChannel + crypto-routing đa-peer longest-prefix (IpPrefix/WireGuardCryptoRouter/WireGuardMultiPeerChannel) (V3.f + V.3)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther SoftEther SSL-VPN: PACK codec (binary typed key-value — list element {name≤63, type int/data/str/unistr/int64, mảng value} big-endian) + helper Set/Get theo tên (V4.a) + control handshake: watermark POST + hello/login codec + auth SHA-0 (secure_password) qua IByteStreamTransport (V4.b) + data plane Ethernet-over-TLS: block frame codec (uint32(n)+{uint32(size)·bytes}) + SoftEtherEthernetChannel (IEthernetChannel) + keep-alive (V4.c) + multi-connection (welcome max_connection/half_connection + additional_connect codec + SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux gộp 1-32 socket = 1 session: round-robin egress + N decode loop, SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner full/half-duplex — V.4) + payload codec (use_compress: SoftEtherPayloadCompressor DEFLATE per-frame magic 0xDEADBEEFCAFEFACE; use_encrypt: SoftEtherEncryptedTransport RC4 per-direction tái dùng Crypto.Rc4 — V.4)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect OpenConnect/AnyConnect (ocserv): CSTP framing 8-byte (STF|len|type — DATA/DPD/KEEPALIVE/DISCONNECT/COMPRESSED/TERMINATE, seam F.2) + HTTP auth config-auth XML (init/form/reply/success + cookie) + HTTP CONNECT /CSCOSSLC/tunnel parse X-CSTP-* + X-DTLS-* → TunnelConfig (V5.a) + CstpChannel (IPacketChannel CSTP-over-TLS) + CstpDatagramChannel/CstpDatagramFraming (IPacketChannel CSTP-over-DTLS, header 1-byte type, 1 datagram=1 gói — V5.c) + OpenConnectHttpTransactor (auth POST/CONNECT byte-exact qua IByteStreamTransport) + CstpDpdState (clock-inject DPD/keepalive) (V5.b) + CstpRekeyState/OpenConnectRekeyMethod (clock-inject rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-Method/-Time, ParsedRekeyMethod None/Ssl/NewTunnel — V5.d)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp     PPTP (RFC 2637): control TCP/1723 codec (SCCRQ/SCCRP, OCRQ/OCRP, Echo, Set-Link-Info, Call-Clear/CDN, Stop-CC — magic 0x1A2B3C4D, big-endian) + reassembler + PptpControlConnection state machine (PNS/client) + CCP/MPPE negotiator (CcpNegotiator trên PppNegotiator, option MPPE RFC 2118/3078) + MppeSessionFactory (ráp MppeSession F.5b từ MS-CHAPv2) + GRE data plane (PptpGreCodec/PptpGreChannel Enhanced GRE §4.1 trên IDatagramTransport proto-47 + MppePppFrameChannel decorator MPPE). OFFLINE code+test (V6.a + V6.b); Drivers.Pptp runtime nay đã build trên F.9 raw-IP, live validate chờ Q.1
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap  IP-in-IP/GRE thuần (TRẦN, không mã hóa) trên IDatagramTransport raw-IP (F.9): GRE chuẩn v0 (RFC 2784/2890 — GreCodec/GreTunnelChannel proto-47, KHÁC Enhanced GRE PPTP) + RawIpPassthroughChannel header-less cho IPIP (proto-4, RFC 2003) & SIT/6in4 (proto-41, RFC 4213) — mỗi loại 1 IPacketChannel (L3). OFFLINE codec+kênh (V.8a); driver/EtherIP/L2TPv3/live chờ V.8 b-c
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
TRANSPORT TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls  DTLS 1.2 client (IDatagramTransport) qua BouncyCastle DtlsClientProtocol — SslStream không làm DTLS; bọc UDP pipe, mã hóa/giải mã từng datagram, cert-callback tùy chọn (F.3 — consumer OpenConnect V5.c, đã wire vào Drivers.OpenConnect)
          TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.RawIp RawIpDatagramTransport (IDatagramTransport) trên raw socket (SocketType.Raw) chở IP protocol tùy ý (ESP-50/GRE-47) không bọc UDP/TCP — đường DUY NHẤT userspace cho proto tùy ý, BẮT BUỘC elevate; IRawIpTransportFactory (interface ở Abstractions) probe quyền thật + ném RawIpNotPermittedException; RawIpv4 strip IPv4 header + drop fragment; best-effort trên Windows (OS/firewall có thể nuốt proto-50) (F.9 — consumer P0.8c native ESP, V6.b GRE, V.8 IP-in-IP)
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
CRYPTO    TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto    AES-CBC/CTR/GCM, ChaCha20-Poly1305, XChaCha20-Poly1305, DH(MODP), HMAC-PRF, TLS1-PRF, anti-replay, MD4, DES; Noise/ (X25519, BLAKE2s, HMAC-BLAKE2s, Noise-KDF, NoiseSymmetricState)
─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
CORE      TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions   interface + model + enum (không phụ thuộc gì)
```

> Project `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Udp` (tầng TRANSPORT cũ) đã **gom vào `Ipsec` dưới `Nat/`** — xem bảng
> [Khác biệt so với design docs](#khác-biệt-so-với-design-docs).

## 3. Hợp đồng cốt lõi (Abstractions)

Chuỗi 3 interface phân cấp là xương sống của toàn bộ thư viện:

| Interface | Vai trò |
|---|---|
| [IVpnProtocolDriver.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnProtocolDriver.cs#L9) | Điểm vào plugin: `Name`, `Capabilities`, `ConnectAsync(endpoint, credentials, ct)` |
| [IVpnConnection.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnConnection.cs#L7) | Một kết nối sống (1 IKE-SA / 1 TLS), sở hữu nhiều `IVpnSession`; `OpenSessionAsync()` |
| [IVpnSession.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Interfaces/IVpnSession.cs#L10) | Một endpoint IP logic: `Config` (IP/DNS/route/MTU) + `PacketChannel` |
| [IPacketChannel.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IPacketChannel.cs#L6) | Kênh L3: `WriteIpPacketAsync()` + event `InboundIpPacket` — "card mạng ảo" mà IP stack bám vào |
| [ILinkChannel.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/ILinkChannel.cs#L9) | Base chung: `Mtu`, `MaxHeaderLength`, `Medium` (Ip/Ethernet), `RequiresLinkAddressResolution` |
| [IEthernetChannel.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IEthernetChannel.cs#L7) | Kênh **L2** (kế thừa `ILinkChannel`): `LinkAddress` (MAC 6 byte), `WriteFrameAsync()` + event `InboundFrame` — **đã có impl** [`EthernetSwitch.Port`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.Port.cs#L14) + [`OpenVpnTapChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) trên nền L2.0–L2.3 (switch học MAC + `VirtualHost` bridge L2↔L3 + ARP IPv4 — xem §5 *Ethernet*/§9); **2 driver L2 tiêu thụ thật bridge 1-host xuống L3**: OpenVPN tap-mode (`OpenVpnTapChannel` → `VirtualHost`+`ArpResolver`, IP từ ifconfig) và **SoftEther** (`SoftEtherEthernetChannel` → `VirtualHost`+`ArpResolver`, IP từ **DHCP** SecureNAT — driver L2 thật đầu tiên có lease, V4.c); **`EthernetAdapter` (L2.7) + `MultiHostSession` (L2.8) nay ráp sẵn multi-host** (N station = N `IVpnSession`) + năng lực driver tap/SoftEther khai báo `L2Ethernet`/`L2BroadcastDomain`/`SupportsMultiHost`; **còn lại** = gắn uplink VPN vào adapter (driver data-plane đa-host) |

Hợp đồng transport phụ trợ: [IByteStreamTransport.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs#L4) — **đã có hiện thực** đầu tiên [`TlsByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp/Transport/TlsByteStream.cs#L23) (driver SSTP, P0.1: đáy TCP/TLS cho SSTP_DUPLEX_POST + PPP-over-stream; project `Transport.Tls` dùng chung là roadmap F.1) — và [IDatagramTransport.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L10) (UDP, chưa có impl; IKE/ESP demux thật ở [`Ipsec/Nat`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat), giữ làm nền DTLS F.3). *(2 hợp đồng `ISecuritySession`/`IPacketEncapsulator` đã **xóa ở P0.1** — shape phân kỳ với `EspSession`/framing thật; sẽ tái thiết kế từ ≥2 consumer thật ở roadmap F.2.)* Seam **resolve outer host**: [IHostResolver.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/IHostResolver.cs#L10) → [DnsHostResolver.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/DnsHostResolver.cs#L14) (literal-passthrough + chọn họ theo [`AddressFamilyPreference`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Net/AddressFamilyPreference.cs); pure `Select` ưu-tiên-1-họ-fallback-họ-kia, testable không cần DNS) — 2 consumer thật: SSTP `TlsByteStream` + L2TP `L2tpIpsecConnection.ResolveAsync` (P1.2).

[VpnDriverCapabilities.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/VpnDriverCapabilities.cs#L9) cho façade
"hỏi năng lực" driver trước khi kết nối — thuộc tính chính: `LinkLayer`, `MultiHostModel`, `TransportKinds`, `SecurityKinds`,
`AuthMethods`, `AddressAssignment`, `UsesPpp`, `RequiresRawIpSocket`, `RequiresElevation`. Các enum năng lực —
[VpnLinkLayer.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/VpnLinkLayer.cs#L4) (L3Ip/L2Ethernet/Both) ·
[MultiHostModel.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/MultiHostModel.cs#L4) (None/RoutedPrefixes/L2BroadcastDomain) ·
[VpnTransportKind.cs:5](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/VpnTransportKind.cs#L5) `[Flags]` (Tcp/Udp/Tls/Dtls/RawIp) ·
[VpnSecurityKind.cs:5](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/VpnSecurityKind.cs#L5) `[Flags]` (Tls/Dtls/Esp/Noise/Mppe) ·
[VpnAuthMethod.cs:5](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/VpnAuthMethod.cs#L5) `[Flags]` (PreSharedKey/Certificate/UserPassword/Eap/Saml/Otp) ·
[AddressAssignment.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Enums/AddressAssignment.cs#L4) (Ipcp/ConfigPush/OutOfBand/Dhcp) —
đa số enum nay đã có **driver tiêu thụ thật** (đủ 7 driver đã wire — xem §4/§6/§7): 2 driver SSTP + L2TP/IPsec khai **L3Ip + UsesPpp +
AddressAssignment=Ipcp** (xem §6/§7), driver **IKEv2-native (V.1)** khai **L3Ip + không-PPP + Esp + AddressAssignment=ConfigPush** (CP cấp IP, ESP tunnel mode); thêm **OpenVPN (V2.h)** L3Ip(tun)/L2Ethernet(tap) + Tls + AEAD/CBC, **WireGuard (V3.f)** L3Ip + Udp + **Noise** + AddressAssignment=OutOfBand, **OpenConnect (V5.x)** L3Ip + Tls/**Dtls** + bare-IP (ConfigPush qua X-CSTP-*), và **SoftEther (V4.c)** L2Ethernet + Tls + AddressAssignment=**Dhcp**. Khi driver cần quyền (RawIp) mà process thiếu → ném [VpnElevationRequiredException.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnElevationRequiredException.cs#L7).
**Phân loại lỗi kết nối**: cây ngoại lệ [VpnConnectionException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnConnectionException.cs#L8) (base, **không** sealed) với 3 lớp con sealed —
[VpnAuthenticationException.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnAuthenticationException.cs#L7) (sai credential: PPP MS-CHAPv2 fail / IKE PSK·HASH_R mismatch),
[VpnServerRejectedException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnServerRejectedException.cs#L8) (server từ chối ở mức giao thức: SSTP Call-Connect-Nak / non-200 handshake / crypto-binding thiếu-hoặc-ngắn / IKE Quick Mode HASH(2) sai hoặc không có SA / **IKE handshake bị gateway từ chối bằng NOTIFY lỗi** NO-PROPOSAL-CHOSEN… — **P0.8a**),
[VpnNetworkTimeoutException.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/VpnNetworkTimeoutException.cs#L8) (transport: socket/TLS/IO fail, IKE no-response **phân loại theo cổng** — im lặng sau float UDP/4500 ⇒ thông điệp nghi **forced-NAT-T** (P0.8a), Quick-Mode-rekey no-response). `OperationCanceledException` do caller hủy **không** bị tái phân loại (xem throw site ở §6/§7).
Model đi kèm: [VpnEndpoint.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/VpnEndpoint.cs#L6) (Host/Port **+ `AddressFamilyPreference`** — chọn họ IP cho outer transport, P1.2),
[VpnCredentials.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/VpnCredentials.cs#L4) (Username/Password + PreSharedKey),
[TunnelConfig.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Drivers/Models/TunnelConfig.cs#L9) (AssignedAddress, PrefixLength=32, **AssignedAddressV6/PrefixLengthV6=64** (P1.1, null nếu không bật IPv6), DnsServers, Routes, Mtu=1400 — chính là `Config` ở bảng trên).

## 4. Điểm vào

[VpnClientBuilder.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L18) đăng ký driver kiểu fluent;
[VpnClient.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L8) tra driver theo tên (qua helper [`ResolveDriver` @ :25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L25)) rồi ủy thác `ConnectAsync`.
Façade nay wire **7 driver**: `UseSstp()` / [`UseSstp(RemoteCertificateValidationCallback)` @ :36](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L36) (callback xác thực cert TLS — **P0.6**; không truyền ⇒ chấp nhận mọi cert) / `UseL2tpIpsec()` / [`UseL2tpIpsec(L2tpIpsecReconnectOptions)` @ :47](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L47) / [`UseL2tpIpsec(reconnect, L2tpIpsecTimeoutOptions)` @ :50](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L50) / `UseIkev2()` / [`UseIkev2(Ikev2ReconnectOptions)` @ :57](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L57) / [`UseIkev2(IkeCertificateTrust, …)` @ :65](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L65) (verify gateway bằng cert RFC 7296 §2.15) / [`UseOpenVpn(OpenVpnProfile)` @ :70](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L70) (+ overload client-cert/cert-callback/reconnect @ :73) / [`UseWireGuard(WireGuardConfig)` @ :78](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L78) (+ overload reconnect @ :81) / [`UseOpenConnect()` @ :89](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L89) (+ overload reconnect @ :92 và `(reconnect, cert-callback, groupSelect)` @ :99) / [`UseSoftEther(string hubName)` @ :107](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L107) (+ overload `SoftEtherSessionParams` @ :110, `(session, reconnect)` @ :113, `(hubName, enableIpv6)` @ :121) đều là wrapper gọi
[`AddDriver(IVpnProtocolDriver)` @ :23](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs#L23) (keyed theo `driver.Name`) — nên driver tự định nghĩa cũng nạp được.
`VpnClient` còn có [`GetCapabilities(protocol)` @ :22](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L22) trả `VpnDriverCapabilities`; **P0.5** gom cả hai về cùng [`ResolveDriver` @ :25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClient.cs#L25) nên `GetCapabilities` và `ConnectAsync` ném **cùng `NotSupportedException`** (kèm danh sách protocol đã đăng ký) khi tra protocol chưa có driver.

```csharp
var vpn  = new VpnClientBuilder().UseSstp().UseL2tpIpsec().Build();
IVpnConnection conn = await vpn.ConnectAsync("l2tp-ipsec", endpoint, creds);
IVpnSession    sess = conn.Sessions[0];

// mở socket chạy TRONG tunnel:
var stack = sess.CreateTcpStack();                       // VpnSessionSocketsExtensions
var tcp   = await VpnTcpClient.ConnectAsync(stack, ip, 80);
Stream s  = tcp.GetStream();                             // cắm thẳng vào HttpClient
```

## 5. Vai trò từng module

| Module | Type chính | Trách nhiệm |
|---|---|---|
| **Crypto** | 6 hợp đồng [Crypto/Interfaces/](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Interfaces/) (`IHashAlgo`/`IBlockCipher`/`IAeadCipher`/`IDhGroup`/`IPrf`/`IIntegrityAlgo`); hiện thực [AesCbcCipher.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AesCbcCipher.cs#L10), [AesCtr.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AesCtr.cs#L9), [AesGcmCipher.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/AesGcmCipher.cs#L18), [ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L18), [XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L14), [ModpDhGroup.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/ModpDhGroup.cs#L12), [HmacPrf.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/HmacPrf.cs#L7)/[HmacIntegrity.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/HmacIntegrity.cs#L7), [PrfPlus.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/PrfPlus.cs#L9), [Tls1Prf.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Tls1Prf.cs#L11), [AntiReplayWindow.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7), [Md4.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Md4.cs#L9), [Sha0.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Sha0.cs#L12), [Des.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Des.cs#L8), [Rc4.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs#L13); **MPPE** [Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs#L18), [Mppe/MppeSession.cs:16](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16); **Noise** [Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15), [Noise/Blake2s.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Blake2s.cs#L12), [Noise/Blake2sKeyedMac.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Blake2sKeyedMac.cs#L11), [Noise/HmacBlake2sPrf.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/HmacBlake2sPrf.cs#L14), [Noise/NoiseKdf.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseKdf.cs#L11), [Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs:21](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21) | Primitive theo hợp đồng (đảo ngược phụ thuộc §1). DH MODP group 2 (1024-bit) + 14 (2048-bit); factory integrity `HmacSha1_96` (key20/ICV12 — IKEv1) & `HmacSha256_128` (key32/ICV16 — IKEv2). `Tls1Prf` = PRF TLS 1.0 (P_MD5⊕P_SHA1, RFC 2246) cho key-method-2 OpenVPN; `AntiReplayWindow` cửa sổ trượt 64-gói (RFC 4303) **dùng chung ESP + OpenVPN**. MD4/DES bắt buộc cho MS-CHAPv2 dù lỗi thời; `Sha0` (FIPS 180 1993 = SHA-1 bỏ ROTL1 ở message schedule, `IHashAlgo` 20B) bắt buộc cho auth password SoftEther (V.4, hash cục bộ không lên wire) — KAT FIPS-180 + đối chiếu khác SHA-1. **MPPE/RC4 (F.5b, nền PPTP V.6)**: `Rc4` (stream cipher KSA/PRGA, RFC 6229 KAT, broken RFC 7465) + `MppeKeyDerivation` (RFC 3078 §7.3 `GetNewKeyFromSHA` SHA-1 + initial-key SHA-only + re-key SHA→RC4-self + strength reduction 40/56/128-bit) + `MppeSession` (1 chiều: RC4 + coherency 12-bit + framing A/B/C/D, stateless re-key-mỗi-gói vs stateful re-key-mỗi-256-gói); MPPE start key suy từ MS-CHAPv2 qua `MsChapV2.DeriveMppe*StartKey` (cờ `isServer` chọn Magic2/Magic3). **MPPE+MS-CHAPv2 đã bị phá** — chỉ tương thích legacy. KAT RFC 3079 §3.5 (MasterKey/StartKey/SessionKey 40/56/128 + "Sample Encrypted Message"). `AesGcmCipher`/`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher` là nơi `#if`: BCL native (`AesGcm` net7+, `ChaCha20Poly1305` net5+) vs BouncyCastle (netstandard2.0); cùng shape AEAD nonce 12B/tag 16B/key 32B (ChaCha20-Poly1305 RFC 8439, dùng cho NCP OpenVPN); `XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher` (draft-irtf-cfrg-xchacha: `HChaCha20` suy subkey rồi ủy quyền `ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`, nonce 24B — dùng cho WireGuard cookie-reply V3.c). **Noise/ (F.4 — nền WireGuard V.3 / Nebula V.7, đã KAT; consumer đầu: [WireGuard](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard) V3.b/c)**: `Curve25519DhGroup` (X25519 RFC 7748, IANA group 31, `IDhGroup`), `Blake2s` (BLAKE2s-256 RFC 7693, `IHashAlgo`), `Blake2sKeyedMac` (keyed BLAKE2s output tùy chỉnh — WG mac1/mac2 16B), `HmacBlake2sPrf` (HMAC-BLAKE2s RFC 2104, `IPrf`), `NoiseKdf` (HKDF RFC 5869 trên HMAC-BLAKE2s), **`NoiseSymmetricState`** (V3.a — Noise spec §5.2 SymmetricState cho `Noise_IKpsk2_25519_ChaCha20Poly1305_BLAKE2s`: `InitializeWireGuard` seed `ck=HASH(CONSTRUCTION)`/`h=HASH(ck‖IDENTIFIER)`, `MixHash`/`MixKey` (Kdf2)/`MixKeyAndHash` (Kdf3, PSK)/`EncryptAndHash`+`DecryptAndHash` (ChaCha20-Poly1305 nonce `0^4‖counter` LE, AAD = `h` hiện tại)/`Split` (Kdf2 → cặp transport key 32B) — class state machine **đối xứng thuần**, không trạng thái mạng; tái dùng nguyên primitive F.4 qua DI `IPrf`/`IHashAlgo`/`IAeadCipher`). Khác `Aead/`: **không** `#if` native — BCL cả 2 TFM đều thiếu X25519/BLAKE2s nên dùng BouncyCastle giống nhau (vì vậy `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` nay là PackageReference **không điều kiện**). |
| **Ipsec.Esp** | [EspSession.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSession.cs#L9), [EspDataPlane.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspDataPlane.cs#L9), [EspTunnelChannel.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspTunnelChannel.cs#L12), [EspCipherSuite.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspCipherSuite.cs#L10) (+ [EspCbcHmacSuite.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspCbcHmacSuite.cs#L11) / [EspGcmSuite.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspGcmSuite.cs#L11)), [AntiReplayWindow.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) (ở Crypto — dùng chung ESP + OpenVPN data channel) | Data-plane IPsec: `Protect`/`TryUnprotect`, sequence dùng [`checked(+1)` @ EspSession:43](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSession.cs#L43) → **OverflowException ở gói thứ 2³²** (backstop; rekey-by-sequence ở `EspDataPlane` bên dưới), chống replay (cửa sổ 64 gói). [`EspDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspDataPlane.cs#L9) là base dùng chung của **cả 2 mode**: giữ SA hiện tại + SA cũ (make-before-break), `ProtectOutbound`/`TryUnprotectInbound`, watermark `RekeyNeeded` quanh 2³². [`EspTunnelChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspTunnelChannel.cs#L12) = ESP **tunnel mode** → `IPacketChannel` (gói IP nguyên gói, NextHeader 4/41, decap demux — data plane IKEv2, **F.8 xong**); `IpsecL2tpTransport` (driver L2TP) là **transport mode** trên cùng base. `EspCipherSuite` là base + 3 factory: `AesCbcHmacSha1` (đường **live** IKEv1), `AesCbcHmacSha256` (mặc định IKEv2), `AesGcm` (RFC 4106 — **nay negotiate được** cả IKEv1+IKEv2); wire `SPI‖Seq‖IV‖ct‖ICV`, encrypt-then-MAC. [`EspSuiteSelection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/EspSuiteSelection.cs#L14) (+ enum [`EspEncryptionAlgorithm`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Esp/Enums/EspEncryptionAlgorithm.cs#L4)) là descriptor "suite đã chọn": ánh xạ thuật toán → độ dài keymat (`EncryptionKeyLengthBytes`+`SecondSliceLengthBytes` = integ-key cho CBC / salt 4B cho GCM) → `EspCipherSuite` qua `BuildSuite`, dùng chung V1 lẫn V2. |
| **Ipsec.Ike.V1** | [IkeV1Client.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Client.cs#L18) + codec [IsakmpMessage.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IsakmpMessage.cs#L11), khóa [IkeV1KeyMaterial.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1KeyMaterial.cs#L12)/[IkeV1Phase2Keys.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Phase2Keys.cs#L10), [IkeV1Cipher.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Cipher.cs#L12), [IkeV1Auth.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Auth.cs#L10), [IkeV1QuickMode.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1QuickMode.cs#L10), [IkeV1NatDetection.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1NatDetection.cs#L12), [IkeV1Proposals.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Proposals.cs#L12), [IkeV1Lifetimes.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Lifetimes.cs#L4) | Bắt tay ISAKMP/IKEv1 cho L2TP: Main Mode (MM1–MM6) + Quick Mode (QM1–QM3) → KEYMAT cho ESP. **Đây là IKE đang chạy thực tế.** Phase 1 đề xuất **AES-CBC + SHA1 + PSK + MODP 2/14**; Phase 2 đề xuất **AES-CBC-256+SHA1 trước, AES-GCM-16-256 sau** (ESP transform id 20). `ProcessQuickMode2`/`ProcessRekeyQuickMode2` **xác thực HASH(2)** của responder (RFC 2409 §5.5 = `prf(SKEYID_a, M-ID‖Ni_b‖payload-sau-HASH)`, hash trên **byte gốc nhận** qua `PayloadChainAfterFirst` — không re-encode nên gateway hợp lệ không bị false-reject; mismatch ⇒ `VpnServerRejectedException`) rồi đọc transform server chọn → lộ `NegotiatedEsp`/`RekeyNegotiatedEsp` (`EspSuiteSelection`); khoan dung suite — chỉ là GCM khi id=20, còn lại fallback CBC, nên VPN Gate vẫn CBC. `IkeV1Cipher` giữ **CBC IV-chaining** (RFC 2409 §5.5: IV Quick Mode/Informational = hash(IV-Phase1-cuối ‖ M-ID)) — lý do mỗi DPD/Delete/rekey có IV riêng. Thêm qua **Informational**: DPD keepalive ([IkeV1Dpd.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Dpd.cs)), Quick Mode rekey (`BuildRekeyQuickMode1/2/3`), Delete teardown ([IkeV1Delete.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Delete.cs)). **Rekey Phase 1 in-place (P1.3)**: client thuần chạy lại Main Mode+Quick Mode dưới một `IkeV1Client` mới (ISAKMP SA mới) — `IsForThisSa` so cookie initiator (8 byte cleartext) để orchestrator tách reply rekey khỏi DPD của SA cũ trên cùng socket. **Phân loại handshake bị từ chối** (P0.8a): `IkeV1Client.TryReadRejectNotify` nhận diện Informational clear-text mang NOTIFY lỗi (type 1–16383, tái dùng `IkeV1Dpd.TryReadNotifyType`) để driver fail-fast thay vì parse nhầm thành reply. |

ESP CHILD_SA chào **2 proposal**: AES-CBC-256+SHA256 (#1) rồi AES-GCM-16-256 (#2) ([`EspProposals`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/IkeProposals.cs)); `ProcessAuthResponse` đọc proposal server chọn → `NegotiatedEsp` + `ChildKeys` đúng độ dài. Hậu-AUTH (F.7): **INFORMATIONAL** (DPD `BuildDeadPeerDetection` + DELETE `BuildDeleteChildSa()`/`BuildDeleteChildSa(spi)` [xóa CHILD_SA cũ theo SPI cụ thể sau rekey, §2.8]/`BuildDeleteIkeSa` + `BuildInformationalResponse`), **CREATE_CHILD_SA** rekey CHILD_SA make-before-break (`BuildRekeyChildSaRequest`/`ProcessRekeyChildSaResponse` → [`ChildSaParameters`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Models/ChildSaParameters.cs#L11)) **và rekey IKE SA** (F.7 3b — `BuildRekeyIkeSaRequest`/`ProcessRekeyIkeSaResponse`: SPI/DH mới, `IkeKeyMaterial.DeriveRekey`=`prf(SK_d_old, g^ir\|Ni\|Nr)` §2.18, swing toàn bộ "current IKE SA" SPI/cipher/SK_d + reset message-id về 0 — Phase-1-equivalent; **trước khi swing chuẩn bị sẵn** INFORMATIONAL+DELETE cho IKE SA cũ mã hóa bằng SK_* cũ → `TakePendingOldIkeSaDelete` cho driver gửi trên SA cũ, §2.18); message-id counter. Payload model: [`ConfigurationPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/ConfigurationPayload.cs#L13) (§3.15) + [`DeletePayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/DeletePayload.cs#L10) (§3.11) + [`EapPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/EapPayload.cs#L11) (§3.16, bọc gói EAP RFC 3748 §4) + [`CertificatePayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/CertificatePayload.cs#L10)/[`CertificateRequestPayload`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/CertificateRequestPayload.cs#L11) (§3.6/§3.7, X.509 DER); VendorId còn lại → [RawPayload.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Payloads/RawPayload.cs#L9). **Responder cert auth** (RFC 7296 §2.15 chữ ký số): `IkeClient.VerifyResponderAuth` parse CERT → `IkeCertificateTrust.IsTrusted` (pin leaf / chain CA) → `IkeSignatureAuth.VerifyResponderSignature` (RSA method 1 cả 2 TFM; ECDSA 9/10/11 net5+) verify trên SignedOctets (dùng chung `IkePskAuth.ComputeSignedOctets`); fail/cert-không-tin/downgrade-PSK ⇒ `VpnServerRejectedException`. **EAP-MSCHAPv2** (RFC 7296 §2.16): `BuildAuthRequestEap` (IKE_AUTH bỏ AUTH ⇒ báo EAP) + `ProcessAuthResponseEap` pump (verify PSK AUTH responder msg4, bơm EAP qua nhiều vòng IKE_AUTH, AUTH cuối bằng **MSK** 2 chiều, CHILD_SA ở exchange cuối) → `EapEstablished`/`EapFailed`; state-machine [`EapMsChapV2Client`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V2/Eap/EapMsChapV2Client.cs#L14) tái dùng codec [`MsChapV2`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs) (Crypto). **Protocol đủ cho driver V.1 IKEv2-native; driver nay consume PSK / EAP-MSCHAPv2 (auth client) + verify responder PSK / cert + multi-TS + gắn timer rekey CHILD_SA và IKE SA, mỗi loại rekey phát DELETE cho SA cũ (không để gateway tự timeout) — còn lại của V.1 là validate live (lab Q.1) + honest-first NAT-T + cert trên đường EAP.** |
| **L2tp** | [L2tpClient.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L13) + [L2tpSession.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpSession.cs#L9) trên [IL2tpTransport.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/IL2tpTransport.cs#L7), [L2tpControlChannel.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpControlChannel.cs#L12), codec [L2tpCodec.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpCodec.cs#L11) | L2TPv2 (RFC 2661): tunnel SCCRQ→SCCRP→SCCCN, session ICRQ→ICRP→ICCN (SCCCN/ICCN tự gửi trong `OnControl`); truyền tin cậy Ns/Nr + ZLB ack + retransmit head-of-line với **exponential backoff+jitter** (1s ×2 tới cap 8s, P1.4) + **cap số lần** (`MaxRetransmits`, 0 = vô hạn; driver L2TP/IPsec đặt 8) → vượt cap raise [`Failed` @ :49](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpControlChannel.cs#L49). **Multi-session (P1.7)**: một tunnel mang **N session** — `ConnectAsync` dựng `PrimarySession`, [`OpenSessionAsync` @ :80](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L80) mở session phụ (best-effort; server từ chối bằng CDN ⇒ exception). Mỗi `L2tpSession` có `LocalSessionId`/`PeerSessionId` + `DataReceived`/`SendDataAsync` riêng; inbound data **demux theo session id**, ICRP/CDN tương quan theo session id ở header (fallback session đang mở khi peer trả 0). `L2tpCodec` serialize header+AVP, phân biệt control (T=1) vs data (T=0). Keepalive `SendHelloAsync` (HELLO); teardown `L2tpSession.SendCallDisconnectAsync` (CDN) + `SendStopControlConnectionAsync` (StopCCN). Event [`Disconnected` @ :59](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L59) (StopCCN/control-fail **hoặc** session chính bị CDN) chính là tín hiệu "L2TP teardown" ở §6.1; [`DataReceived` @ :56](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.L2tp/L2tpClient.cs#L56) là PPP inbound của session chính. |

[Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs:15](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) | Protocol OpenVPN thuần (community server) **không PPP**. **V2.a+config+V2.b xong**: (1) codec gói control — byte đầu = 5-bit opcode + 3-bit key_id (`Header`/`ReadOpcode`/`ReadKeyId`), gói control = `session_id(8)` + ACK array (`ack_len(1)` + `4·M` packet-id + `remote_session_id(8)` nếu M>0) + `packet_id(4)` + payload TLS (P_ACK_V1 bỏ 2 trường cuối); `EncodeControl`/`TryDecodeControl`. (2) **reliability state machine** (clock inject, tất định): `OpenVpnReliableSendWindow` (gán packet-id từ 0 + in-flight window + `CollectDue(nowMs)` gửi/retransmit backoff + `Acknowledge` + `IsExhausted`), `OpenVpnReliableReceiveWindow` (dedup + buffer lệch-thứ-tự + `TryDeliver` in-order cho TLS + `TakeAcks` ≤8/≤4), policy `OpenVpnReliabilityOptions` (mirror `L2tpRetransmitOptions`). (3) **config**: [`OpenVpnProfile`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Config/OpenVpnProfile.cs#L11) (model lập trình driver tiêu thụ — remote(s)/proto/device/TLS material/cipher/auth/options + `OtherDirectives` raw) + [`OpenVpnConfigParser`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Config/OpenVpnConfigParser.cs#L13) `Parse(text)` đọc `.ovpn` **thuần text→model không I/O** (cert/key inline `<ca>…</ca>` → PEM, dạng path → `FilePath`; bỏ comment, arg trong `"…"`, flatten `<connection>`, inline thắng path). (4) **V2.b TLS-in-control**: `OpenVpnControlChannel` (client) ráp 2 reliability window + codec + session-id (64-bit random) + transport `IOpenVpnTransport`, `ConnectAsync` làm reset HARD_RESET_CLIENT_V2 ⇄ HARD_RESET_SERVER_V2 (packet-id 0) rồi `SslStream` AuthenticateAsClient trên `OpenVpnTlsBridgeStream` in-memory (write TLS → fragment ≤1200 + backpressure theo window; read ← payload in-order); pump acks piggyback ≤4 / P_ACK riêng ≤8 + retransmit theo timer; lộ `TlsStream` cho V2.d. (5) **V2.c wrap control packet** (opt-in `IOpenVpnControlWrap` ở ctor; null = gửi verbatim): [`OpenVpnStaticKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnStaticKey.cs#L17) parse `ta.key` 2048-bit (16 dòng×32 hex = `key2`: 2 bộ `cipher[64]\|hmac[64]`); [`OpenVpnTlsAuthWrap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnTlsAuthWrap.cs#L19) (`--tls-auth`) bọc HMAC (mặc định SHA1, dùng được SHA256…) — wire `op\|sid\|HMAC\|replay_id(4)\|net_time(4)\|body`, HMAC = `H(K_out, replay_id\|net_time\|op\|sid\|body)`, key theo `OpenVpnKeyDirection` (client = Inverse/Bidirectional); [`OpenVpnTlsCryptWrap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnTlsCryptWrap.cs#L21) (`--tls-crypt`) xác thực **+ mã hóa** cố định HMAC-SHA256 + AES-256-CTR (tái dùng [`AesCtr`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AesCtr.cs)) — wire `op\|sid\|packet_id(8)\|tag(32)\|E(body)`, tag = `HMAC256(Ka, op\|sid\|packet_id\|body)`, IV = `tag[0..16]`, hướng cố định theo role (client out=set1/in=set0); cả 2 bọc **mọi** gói control kể cả HARD_RESET, unwrap thất bại ⇒ drop datagram. Codec là byte→byte quanh `EncodeControl`/`TryDecodeControl` (decode/state-machine không đổi). (6) **V2.d key-method-2 + data channel AEAD**: sau handshake, client gửi key-method-2 message trên `TlsStream` (`uint32 0 \| key_method=2 \| key_source2(pre-master 48 + 2×random 32) \| P_string options/user/pass`) rồi đọc reply server (random×2 + options), [`OpenVpnKeyMethod2.DeriveDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L122) suy khóa bằng [`Tls1Prf`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Tls1Prf.cs#L11) (master secret 48 → key2 256B, layout `key2` tái dùng `OpenVpnStaticKey`), **hướng key SỬA BUG**: [`SliceDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L108) nay đúng `isServer ? (1,0) : (0,1)` ⇒ **client out=set0/in=set1** (server ngược) — trước đảo nửa key2 (out=set1/in=set0) nên data không chạy live; **đã kiểm chứng live** với OpenVPN server thật (VPN Gate) → [`OpenVpnDataChannelKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataChannelKeys.cs#L9) (cipher key 32 + implicit IV 8 mỗi chiều); [`OpenVpnKeyNegotiation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyNegotiation.cs#L9) chạy trao đổi đó trên stream (hook [`OpenVpnControlChannel.NegotiateKeyMaterialAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs#L149)). **Data channel sau interface [`IOpenVpnDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/IOpenVpnDataChannel.cs#L10)** (`Protect`/`TryUnprotect`/`SentPacketCount`) với **2 hiện thực** dùng chung wrapper [`OpenVpnDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataPlane.cs#L11): (a) **AEAD** [`OpenVpnDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataChannel.cs#L22) gói **AES/ChaCha-GCM** (tái dùng [`AesGcmCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/AesGcmCipher.cs)): wire `op\|key_id(1)\|[peer_id(3)]\|packet_id(4)\|tag(16)\|ct`, nonce = `packet_id ‖ implicit_iv(8)`, AAD = header rõ; (b) **non-AEAD CBC** [`OpenVpnCbcDataChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcDataChannel.cs#L23) (cipher một server NCP-less như OpenVPN function của SoftEther dùng — AES-128/192/256-CBC + HMAC `--auth`): wire `op\|key_id(1)\|[peer_id(3)]\|HMAC(full)\|IV(16)\|AES-CBC(PKCS7(packet_id(4)‖payload))`, HMAC phủ `IV‖ct` (prepend, so hằng-thời-gian), packet-id 4B **trong** envelope mã hóa (IV random/gói) — [`OpenVpnCbcCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcCipher.cs#L12) catalog AES-CBC + [`OpenVpnDataAuth`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataAuth.cs#L12) map `--auth`→HMAC full-digest SHA1/256/384/512/MD5, key [`OpenVpnCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCbcDataKeys.cs#L9) cắt qua [`SliceCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMethod2.cs#L132)/[`OpenVpnKeyMaterial.DeriveCbcDataKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeyMaterial.cs#L29) (cipher key + HMAC key từ key2). **P_DATA_V1 vs V2**: cả 2 channel có tham số `dataV2` (gửi V2 có peer-id 3B / V1 không peer-id 1B); **nhận tự phát hiện theo opcode** (DataV2→header 4B, DataV1→header 1B) nên dung nạp cả hai; cả 2 đều packet-id `checked(++)` (overflow ⇒ phải rekey) + cửa sổ chống replay 64-gói ([`AntiReplayWindow`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) ở Crypto). (7) **V2.e config-pull + keepalive + make-before-break**: [`OpenVpnControlMessage`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnControlMessage.cs#L10) build/read control string NUL-terminated trên `TlsStream` (text — không có 4-byte sentinel như key-method); [`OpenVpnControlChannel.RequestConfigAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs#L164) gửi `PUSH_REQUEST` đọc `PUSH_REPLY` → [`OpenVpnPushReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPushReply.cs#L14) parse `ifconfig`/`route`/`dhcp-option DNS`/`peer-id`/`ping`/`ping-restart`/`cipher`/`topology` → `ToTunnelConfig` (subnet→prefix từ netmask, net30→/30); keepalive [`OpenVpnPing`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPing.cs#L8) magic 16B (gói data) + [`OpenVpnKeepalive`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeepalive.cs#L11) timing clock-inject (`ShouldSendPing`/`IsPeerDead`); [`OpenVpnDataPlane`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataPlane.cs#L11) **mirror `EspDataPlane`** giữ current + previous data channel (soft-reset rekey không mất gói in-flight), `RekeyNeeded` quanh 2³² packet-id. (8) **V2.f NCP + compression stub**: [`OpenVpnDataCipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnDataCipher.cs#L12) catalog (AES-256-GCM/AES-128-GCM/**CHACHA20-POLY1305**, `TryResolve` theo tên, `TryResolveServerList`/`ExtractIvCiphers` đọc `IV_CIPHERS` server đẩy ngược, `AdvertisedList`, key size + factory AEAD); [`OpenVpnPeerInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPeerInfo.cs#L16) build `IV_*` (IV_PROTO/IV_NCP=2/**IV_CIPHERS**) cho key-method-2 — cấu hình qua [`OpenVpnPeerInfoOptions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnPeerInfo.cs#L85) (**push-peer-info nâng cao**: IV_PLAT auto-detect linux/win/mac + **IV_MTU** (driver bơm tun MTU) + informational IV_PLAT_VER/IV_SSL_VER/IV_GUI_VER + user-vars `UV_*` qua `Extra`); suy khóa tách **cipher-independent** `DeriveKey2` → `SliceDataKeys(key2, cipher, isServer)` để chốt cipher **sau PUSH_REPLY** (`OpenVpnKeyMaterial` giữ key2; `OpenVpnKeyNegotiation`/`NegotiateKeyMaterialAsync` trả material), `OpenVpnDataChannel` tự-chọn AES-GCM theo độ dài khóa (16/128, 32/256); [`OpenVpnCompression`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnCompression.cs#L11) framing **stub** (None/CompLzo 1-byte 0xFA/StubV2 zero-overhead) — chỉ chào no-compression, gói thật-sự-nén ⇒ reject. **CHACHA20-POLY1305** (RFC 8439, [`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L18) shim BCL native net5+ / BouncyCastle ns2.0) đã vào catalog + IV_CIPHERS, cả 3 AEAD chạy thật ở data channel (driver truyền `cipher.CreateCipher()`). (9) **V2.g transport TCP + tap-mode**: [`OpenVpnTcpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTcpFraming.cs#L15) framing 16-bit big-endian length cho stream transport (`Encode` egress + decoder `Append`/`TryReadPacket` ráp lại gói qua mọi ranh đọc — hiện thực OpenVPN của seam F.2 `IPacketEncapsulator`), [`OpenVpnTcpTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTcpTransport.cs#L14) bọc [`IByteStreamTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs) (F.1 — TCP/TLS) thành `IOpenVpnTransport` (`SendAsync` length-prefix + write nối tiếp; `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc→ráp→`DatagramReceived`); cầu nối **device-link** [`OpenVpnDataLink`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnDataLink.cs#L15) (compression-frame + `OpenVpnDataPlane.Protect`/`TryUnprotect` ↔ sink transport) với 2 hiện thực: [`OpenVpnTunChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTunChannel.cs#L12) (`dev tun` → L3 `IPacketChannel`, payload = gói IP, MaxHeaderLength 0) + [`OpenVpnTapChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnTapChannel.cs#L15) (`dev tap` → L2 `IEthernetChannel` cắm fabric Ethernet, payload = khung Ethernet, MaxHeaderLength 14 + MAC + resolution) — wire data channel **y hệt**, chỉ khác nội dung payload + medium kênh. **(10) V2.h transport UDP + driver**: [`OpenVpnUdpTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnUdpTransport.cs#L13) bọc [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs) (UDP) thành `IOpenVpnTransport` — 1 datagram = 1 gói nên **không framing** (sibling UDP của `OpenVpnTcpTransport`); 0-byte không phải EOF. `OpenVpnDataLink.TryReceivePayload` nay **drop gói ping** (`OpenVpnPing.IsPing`) sau giải mã+de-compress để keepalive không lọt vào IP/Ethernet layer. Driver `Drivers.OpenVpn` ráp tất cả thành tunnel chạy thật (xem bảng **Drivers.OpenVpn** ở §5). **(11) V.2-occ** (offline): [`OpenVpnClientCertificate`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/Helpers/OpenVpnClientCertificate.cs#L26) nạp `cert`/`key` (PEM inline hoặc path) → `X509Certificate2` có private key (net5+ `CreateFromPem`→PKCS#12; ns2.0 BouncyCastle PEM→PKCS#12); [`OpenVpnControlChannel.SendExitNotifyAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/OpenVpnControlChannel.cs) gửi explicit-exit-notify (`EXIT_NOTIFY`) best-effort + lộ `ServerKeyMethodOptions` (NCP-less mining IV_CIPHERS). **Chưa**: `tls-ekm` (F.5a — scaffold interface [`ITlsKeyingMaterialExporter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/ITlsKeyingMaterialExporter.cs) khai báo nhưng **chưa hiện thực**: `SslStream` net8/ns2.0 không có RFC 5705 exporter — đã kiểm bằng reflection; `ExportKeyingMaterial` chỉ có net9+ / cần BouncyCastle TLS); **soft-reset make-before-break** (hiện rekey bằng re-establish). **Validate live (đã chạy thật)**: tunnel tun/UDP tới OpenVPN server VPN Gate (AES-128-CBC, server NCP-less, P_DATA_V1) lên + HTTP GET checkip trả IP công cộng + UDP DNS + ICMP đều chạy 2 chiều; **còn lại — gói lớn/MTU**: payload lớn (TLS ServerHello của https) chưa qua được, nghi cần MTU/MSS clamp cho path qua VPN (liên quan Q.4). **Data plane server-role chỉ trong test.** (xem [`11`](11-todo-roadmap.md) §V.2 + [`06`](06-openvpn.md)). |

mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply + V3.d data channel type-4 + V3.e timers/state machine + V3.f config tĩnh/channel xong** (consumer đầu của Noise/ F.4 + V3.a). (1) [`WireGuardConstants`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardConstants.cs#L17) — `CONSTRUCTION`/`IDENTIFIER` re-export từ [`NoiseSymmetricState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21) (single source, không lệch) + `LABEL_MAC1`/`LABEL_COOKIE` (chờ V3.c) + kích thước (`KeyLength`32/`TagLength`16/`TimestampLength`12/`MacLength`16/`IndexLength`4) + message type 1–4 + `InitiationMessageLength`148/`ResponseMessageLength`92. (2) [`WireGuardTai64n`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardTai64n.cs#L19) — `Now()`/`Encode(instant)` ra TAI64N 12B (8B giây TAI base `0x400000000000000A` big-endian + 4B nanosecond big-endian) + `Compare` lexicographic đơn điệu (responder chỉ kiểm timestamp tăng nghiêm ngặt). (3) [`WireGuardMessageCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardMessageCodec.cs#L13) — `EncodeInitiation`/`TryDecodeInitiation` (type-1 148B) + `EncodeResponse`/`TryDecodeResponse` (type-2 92B) + `EncodeCookieReply`/`TryDecodeCookieReply` (type-3 64B) đúng từng byte: type byte + 3 reserved zero + index 32-bit **little-endian** + ephemeral 32 + AEAD field; length/type sai ⇒ `false` (drop). V3.c thêm `ApplyMacs`/`VerifyMac1`/`ReadMac1` thao tác mac1/mac2 **in-place** trên buffer đã encode (offset suy từ độ dài: mac1 = cuối−32, mac2 = cuối−16, dùng chung type-1/2). (4) [`WireGuardHandshake`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardHandshake.cs#L23) — state machine **đối xứng thuần** 1 phía (initiator `CreateInitiation`→`ConsumeResponse`, responder `ConsumeInitiation`→`CreateResponse`, `DeriveTransportKeys` Split + hoán đổi theo role để `send`bên-này = `recv`bên-kia); chỉ **xếp thứ tự** mix/DH/AEAD đúng whitepaper §5.4, tái dùng nguyên [`NoiseSymmetricState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/NoiseSymmetricState.cs#L21) (`InitializeWireGuard`/`MixHash`/`MixKey`/`MixKeyAndHash`/`EncryptAndHash`/`DecryptAndHash`/`Split`) + [`Curve25519DhGroup`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Noise/Curve25519DhGroup.cs#L15) (X25519) + [`ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/ChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L18) qua DI; mỗi `KDF1(ck,x)` whitepaper hiện thực bằng `MixKey` (KDF2) — output đầu (chaining key) giống hệt, cipher key thừa luôn bị ghi đè trước AEAD kế; bước PSK `KDF3` là `MixKeyAndHash`. Sai tag/PSK ⇒ `ConsumeInitiation`/`ConsumeResponse` trả `false`. (5) **V3.c mac1/mac2 + cookie-reply (DoS, whitepaper §5.4.4/§5.4.7)** — [`WireGuardMac`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardMac.cs#L22) keyed-BLAKE2s-128: `ForRecipient(pub)` tiền-hash `mac1Key=HASH(LABEL_MAC1‖pub)`/`CookieKey=HASH(LABEL_COOKIE‖pub)`, `ComputeMac1`/`VerifyMac1` + `ComputeMac2`/`VerifyMac2` (cookie-keyed), so sánh **constant-time** (tự cài cho cả ns2.0); [`WireGuardCookie`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/WireGuardCookie.cs#L21) `ComputeCookie(secret,addr)=MAC(secret,addr)` + `CreateReply` (responder seal cookie bằng [`XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Aead/XChaCha20Poly1305Cipher.cs#L14), nonce 24B, AAD = mac1 gói kích hoạt) / `TryReadCookie` (initiator mở, sai ⇒ false). `WireGuardHandshake` gắn wire layer: `StampOutgoingMacs` (stamp mac1 key-peer + mac2 nếu có cookie, lưu mac1 vừa gửi), `VerifyIncomingMac1` (verify key-self, drop nếu sai), `CreateCookieReply`/`ConsumeCookieReply` (cache cookie → mac2 lần kế). (6) **V3.d data channel type-4 (whitepaper §5.4.6)** — [`WireGuardDataCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardDataCodec.cs#L17) dựng/đọc gói transport-data 16B header `type(1)|reserved(3)|receiver(4 LE)|counter(8 LE)` + AEAD output (ciphertext‖tag16); `WriteNonce` ra nonce 12B = `0^4‖counter(8 LE)`; length/type/reserved sai ⇒ `false` (drop). [`WireGuardTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs#L24) stateful theo cặp [`WireGuardTransportKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Handshake/Models/WireGuardTransportKeys.cs#L11) từ Split: `Seal` (ChaCha20-Poly1305 nonce counter-LE, **AAD rỗng**, counter u64 đơn điệu **từ 0**, overflow ⇒ ném — rekey trước), `TryOpen` (kiểm receiver-index của mình → anti-replay → AEAD; sai ⇒ drop), `Keepalive` = `Seal(empty)` (payload 0). [`WireGuardReplayProtector`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardReplayProtector.cs#L19) chống replay 64-gói **trên counter u64 đầy đủ**: **tái dùng** [`AntiReplayWindow`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/AntiReplayWindow.cs#L7) cho 32-bit thấp (ánh xạ counter-0-based → window-1-based bằng `low+1`) trong một epoch high-32, tự theo dõi high-32 (epoch tiến ⇒ reset window; epoch cũ ⇒ replay) — vì `AntiReplayWindow` là `uint` còn WG counter là `u64`. (7) **V3.e timers + state machine (whitepaper §6.2)** — [`WireGuardTimers`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardTimers.cs#L14) hằng timer ở **ms**: `RekeyAfterTimeMs`120s/`RejectAfterTimeMs`180s/`RekeyAttemptTimeMs`90s/`RekeyTimeoutMs`5s/`KeepaliveTimeoutMs`10s + `RekeyAfterMessages`(2⁶⁰)/`RejectAfterMessages`(2⁶⁴−2¹³−1) + `PersistentKeepaliveMs`(0=tắt mặc định), bất biến + override cho test + `Default`. [`WireGuardPeerState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/WireGuardPeerState.cs#L22) state machine **clock-inject** (mirror [`OpenVpnKeepalive`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenVpn/DataChannel/OpenVpnKeepalive.cs#L11): mỗi quyết định nhận `nowMs`): ghi sự kiện `OnHandshakeInitiated`/`OnHandshakeCompleted`/`OnDataSent`/`OnDataReceived`/`Reset`; quyết định **thuần** `NeedsHandshake`/`NeedsRekey`(t≥120s hoặc đếm gói)/`IsSessionDead`(t≥180s hoặc đếm gói)/`ShouldResendHandshake`(REKEY_TIMEOUT 5s+jitter inject)/`ShouldAbandonHandshake`(REKEY_ATTEMPT_TIME 90s)/`ShouldSendKeepalive`(persistent đúng nhịp + passive sau nhận data 10s) + `Evaluate(nowMs)` chọn 1 [`WireGuardSessionAction`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Enums/WireGuardSessionAction.cs#L8) theo độ khẩn (abandon>resend; initiate>dead>keepalive); không giữ key/crypto, không thread-safe (driver gọi từ 1 timer/IO loop). (8) **V3.f config tĩnh + channel** — [`WireGuardConfig`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Config/WireGuardConfig.cs#L20) (private key, address/DNS, MTU 1420) **single-peer** qua trường tiện ích (`PeerPublicKey?`/`PresharedKey?`/`AllowedIps`/`PersistentKeepaliveSeconds`) **hoặc multi-peer** qua `Peers` (`IReadOnlyList<`[`WireGuardPeer`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Config/WireGuardPeer.cs#L12)`>`) + `EnumeratePeers()` chuẩn hóa + `ToTunnelConfig()` → `TunnelConfig` **tĩnh** (không IPCP/DHCP, routes = hợp allowed-ips mọi peer); [`WireGuardChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Transport/WireGuardChannel.cs#L24) `IPacketChannel` (Medium=Ip, MaxHeaderLength=0) bọc một [`WireGuardTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/DataChannel/WireGuardTransport.cs#L24): `WriteIpPacketAsync` = Seal+send, `Deliver` = TryOpen→raise (drop keepalive rỗng), `SendKeepaliveAsync`; callback `onPacketSealed`/`onPacketReceived` cho driver bơm timer. (9) **V.3 multi-peer crypto-routing** — [`IpPrefix`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/IpPrefix.cs#L18) value-object CIDR thuần (`TryParse` net/prefix|host, mask host-bits, `Contains` so bit, lệch family ⇒ false), [`IpPacketDestination`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/IpPacketDestination.cs#L13) đọc dest từ goi IP v4 (offset 16)/v6 (offset 24) — tối thiểu, **không kéo IpStack** vào project protocol, [`WireGuardCryptoRouter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Routing/WireGuardCryptoRouter.cs#L18) bảng route bất biến `Build(per-peer allowed-ips)` + `TryRoute(dest)` **longest-prefix** → peer index (tie = peer thêm trước; không phủ ⇒ false), [`WireGuardMultiPeerChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.WireGuard/Transport/WireGuardMultiPeerChannel.cs#L25) `IPacketChannel` ổn định trước N `WireGuardChannel`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` route dest → peer (single-peer ⇒ peer 0 không cần parse IP), `SetPeerChannel(i, ch)` hot-swap channel 1 peer (rekey, peer khác giữ nguyên), `Deliver(span)` thử từng peer channel → index peer mở được (gói inbound gán về peer đó) hoặc −1, `onNoRoute` báo drop (`VpnDropReason.NoRoute`). I/O socket + handshake loop đa-peer nằm ở driver `Drivers.WireGuard` (V3.f). **Thuần protocol, không server; interop với WireGuard thật chờ lab Q.1.** (xem [`11`](11-todo-roadmap.md) §V.3). |

`DeflateStream` cả 2 TFM) + [`SoftEtherEncryptedTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L22) (decorator `IByteStreamTransport` áp RC4 keystream **per-direction** dưới block framing, tái dùng [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs); khóa suy từ session key + nhãn hướng); thứ tự **compress-rồi-encrypt** (mặc định tắt — payload thô trên TLS). status ≠200 ⇒ `UnauthorizedAccessException`. **(V5.b data plane)** [`CstpChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpChannel.cs#L24) = `IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-TLS bọc `IByteStreamTransport` + `CstpFraming`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` đóng khung DATA → ghi (serialise qua semaphore), `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc stream→`Append`/`TryReadPacket` demux (DATA/COMPRESSED→`InboundIpPacket`, DPD-REQ→event reply, DISCONNECT/TERMINATE→`PeerClosed`), event `PacketSent`/`PacketReceived`/`DpdRequestReceived` cho driver bơm timer; [`DtlsDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28) bọc một inner `IDatagramTransport` (UDP plaintext): `ConnectAsync` chạy handshake DTLS 1.2 client (pin `ProtocolVersion.DTLSv12`, chào AEAD ECDHE/DHE-RSA+ECDSA+RSA-KT AES-GCM trong [`DefaultDtlsClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DefaultDtlsClient.cs#L15)), sau đó `SendAsync`/`ReceiveAsync` = 1 DTLS record mã hóa/giải mã (giữ ranh giới datagram giống UDP — drop-in thay UDP thô); phơi `SendLimit`/`ReceiveLimit`; `DisposeAsync` gửi close_notify. Cert server validate/pin qua tùy chọn [`DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs#L15) (null⇒accept all; reject⇒`TlsFatalAlert`); client **anonymous** (không cert client). Record layer BouncyCastle **đồng bộ** → cầu sync↔async [`BouncyCastleDatagramBridge`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs#L19) (vòng nền pull inbound vào `BlockingCollection`; `Receive(...,waitMillis)` timeout⇒`-1` cho retransmit timer DTLS; `Send` đồng bộ), handshake + mỗi send/receive offload `Task.Run`; chịu **1 sender + 1 receiver** đồng thời (như socket thô). **Refs CHỈ Abstractions** + PackageReference `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` 2.4.0 (không điều kiện). **Consumer:** OpenConnect V5.c (chưa wire). Test offline dựng **server DTLS giả lập** (`DtlsServerProtocol` + cert RSA self-signed) qua loopback datagram in-memory: handshake + round-trip 2 chiều + cert-callback + reject-cert-abort + **record loss** (drop flight⇒retransmit) + **reorder**. |
| **Pptp** *(V6.a control + CCP/MPPE, offline)* | [PptpControlCodec.cs:22](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlCodec.cs#L22), [PptpControlConnection.cs:22](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlConnection.cs#L22), [Models/PptpControlHeader.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Models/PptpControlHeader.cs#L14), [Enums/PptpControlMessageType.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Enums/PptpControlMessageType.cs#L7), [Ccp/MppeConfigOption.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeConfigOption.cs#L19), [Ccp/CcpNegotiator.cs:22](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/CcpNegotiator.cs#L22), [Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs:20](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs#L20) | **V6.a PPTP control plane + CCP/MPPE negotiate offline xong** (re-implement RFC 2637 + behavior poptop/accel-ppp, **không copy GPL**). (1) **Control codec TCP/1723** [`PptpControlCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlCodec.cs#L22): header chung 12-byte `Length(2 BE)·MsgType(2)·MagicCookie(4=0x1A2B3C4D)·CtrlMsgType(2)·Reserved0(2)` + body big-endian/ASCII NUL-pad cho mọi message (SCCRQ/SCCRP 156B §2.1/2.2, OCRQ 168B §2.7, OCRP 32B §2.8, Echo-Req 16B/Reply 20B §2.5/2.6, Set-Link-Info 24B §2.15, Call-Clear 16B §2.12, CDN 148B §2.13, Stop-CC 16B §2.3/2.4); `Encode(IPptpControlMessage)`/`Decode(packet)` + reassembler instance `Append`+`TryReadMessage` ráp gói qua mọi ranh đọc TCP; magic sai/length-mismatch ⇒ `FormatException`. (2) **State machine** [`PptpControlConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlConnection.cs#L22) (PNS/client trên `IByteStreamTransport`): `EstablishControlConnectionAsync` (SCCRQ→SCCRP), `PlaceOutgoingCallAsync` (OCRQ→OCRP, ghi `PeerCallId`=GRE Call-ID), `SendEchoRequestAsync`/`SendSetLinkInfoAsync`, `ClearCallAsync` (Call-Clear→CDN), `StopControlConnectionAsync`; `ReadMessageAsync` **auto-reply Echo-Request**; refuse Result-Code≠Successful ⇒ `InvalidOperationException`; `PptpControlState` Idle→…→CallEstablished→Closed. (3) **CCP/MPPE** [`CcpNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/CcpNegotiator.cs#L22) **kế thừa [`PppNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L11) dùng chung** (RFC 1962): offer option MPPE đơn (RFC 2118/3078 type 18, 4-byte supported-bits), `OnNak` adopt cường độ server pin, `EvaluatePeerRequest` cap về cường độ tối đa + pin đúng 1 bit, `OnReject`⇒`NotSupportedException`; [`MppeConfigOption`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeConfigOption.cs#L19) codec 4-byte ↔ [`MppeKeyStrength`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/Enums/MppeKeyStrength.cs)/stateless; [`MppeSessionFactory.CreateClientSessions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs#L28) ráp cặp [`MppeSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16) (F.5b) từ MS-CHAPv2 (`DeriveMppeMasterKey`/asymmetric Send-Receive start key RFC 3079) + kết quả CCP — phủ test interop encrypt/decrypt 2 chiều 40/56/128-bit + stateless. **Thêm `PppProtocol.Ccp`=0x80FD/`Compressed`=0x00FD** ở Ppp. **V6.b GRE data plane xong** (code+test offline): [`PptpGreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreCodec.cs#L21)/[`PptpGrePacket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGrePacket.cs#L11) (Enhanced GRE RFC 2637 §4.1, Key high=payload-len/low=Call ID, seq/ack tùy chọn) + [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) (`IPppFrameChannel` trên `IDatagramTransport` proto-47, lọc `localCallId`, seq tăng/ack piggyback §4.4, receive-loop kiểu native-ESP) + [`MppePppFrameChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppePppFrameChannel.cs#L23) (decorator MPPE chạy CCP nội bộ giữa `PppEngine` ↔ GRE). **Driver runtime trên F.9 raw-IP nay đã build (Drivers.Pptp); validate live chờ Q.1 (elevate).** **MS-CHAPv2+MPPE/RC4 đã bị phá — chỉ tương thích legacy.** |
| **Ppp** | [PppEngine.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppEngine.cs#L14) trên [IPppFrameChannel.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Interfaces/IPppFrameChannel.cs#L7); negotiate [PppNegotiator.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L11) (base) → [LcpNegotiator.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/LcpNegotiator.cs#L10)/[IpcpNegotiator.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/IpcpNegotiator.cs#L12)/[Ipv6cpNegotiator.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6cpNegotiator.cs#L14); auth [IPppAuthenticator.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Interfaces/IPppAuthenticator.cs#L9) → [MsChapV2Authenticator.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Auth/MsChapV2Authenticator.cs#L12) (codec [MsChapV2.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs#L11) ở Crypto, dùng chung với IKEv2 EAP); framing [HdlcFramer.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Framing/HdlcFramer.cs#L7)/[HdlcDecoder.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Framing/HdlcDecoder.cs#L7) | Engine chạy **LCP → MS-CHAPv2 → IPCP** (demux theo protocol field dưới 1 lock), event `LinkUp`/`AuthSucceeded`/`AuthFailed`. LCP chỉ chấp nhận MS-CHAPv2 (0xC223+0x81), reject auth khác; IPCP xin IP 0.0.0.0+DNS, nhận qua Configure-Nak; `MsChapV2Authenticator` là nơi `DeriveHlak()` (cho crypto binding SSTP). **IPV6CP (RFC 5072) opt-in** (`enableIpv6`): `Ipv6cpNegotiator` thương lượng Interface-Identifier → link-local `fe80::/64`, chạy song song IPCP + event `Ipv6Up`/`AssignedAddressV6`, **không** đổi link-up IPv4 (mặc định tắt); **nay đã wire vào 2 driver SSTP/L2TP** (opt-in `enableIpv6`) → `TunnelConfig.AssignedAddressV6` (P1.1). Data plane **multiplex hai họ trên một `IPacketChannel`**: `SendIpAsync` chọn PPP Protocol theo version nibble (0x0021 IPv4 / 0x0057 IPv6), inbound demux `Ip`+`Ipv6` cùng đổ về [PppPacketChannel.cs:10](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppPacketChannel.cs#L10) để `TcpIpStack` dual-stack tách lại. Có sẵn **chế độ server** (assignPeer*) — chỉ dùng cho loopback test. HDLC chỉ dùng cho đường SSTP. **Global IPv6 over PPP (P1.1, namespace `Ipv6/`)**: sau IPV6CP (link-local), [`PppIpv6Autoconfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/PppIpv6Autoconfigurator.cs#L20) (impl [`IPppIpv6Autoconfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/IPppIpv6Autoconfigurator.cs#L15)) gửi Router Solicitation, nhận RA (SLAAC) hoặc DHCPv6 trên kênh PPP để suy địa chỉ **global** = prefix ‖ IID (IID = 64 bit thấp của link-local IPV6CP); best-effort (không RA ⇒ null, giữ link-local). Tái dùng engine NDISC/SLAAC/DHCPv6 của Ethernet (`NdiscResolver`/`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`) qua adapter [`PppEthernetChannelAdapter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Ipv6/PppEthernetChannelAdapter.cs#L26) (trình diễn `IPacketChannel` L3 thành `IEthernetChannel`: gửi bỏ 14 byte Ethernet header → `WriteIpPacketAsync`, nhận IPv6 thuần → raise `InboundFrame`; MAC tổng hợp chỉ cosmetic) + option [`Ipv6AddressConfiguratorOptions.InterfaceIdentifierOverride`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfiguratorOptions.cs#L28) (SLAAC dùng IID của link thay vì EUI-64 từ MAC). **Ppp nay ref Ethernet** (acyclic — Ethernet chỉ ref Abstractions). |
| **IpStack** | [TcpIpStack.cs:19](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L19), [TcpConnection.cs:28](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L28), [TcpRetransmitOptions.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpRetransmitOptions.cs#L14), [UdpConnection.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Udp/UdpConnection.cs#L12); codec [Ipv4.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4.cs#L6)/[Ipv4Reassembler.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4Reassembler.cs#L12)/[Ipv6.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6.cs)/[Ipv6Reassembler.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6Reassembler.cs#L12)/[IpLayer.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IpLayer.cs)/[TcpSegment.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpSegment.cs#L7)/[UdpDatagram.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/UdpDatagram.cs#L6)/[Icmpv4.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Icmpv4.cs#L7)/[Icmpv6.cs:7](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Icmpv6.cs#L7), [TcpState.cs:4](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/Enums/TcpState.cs#L4) | TCP/IP userspace **dual-stack**: demux inbound theo **version-nibble** (4→IPv4 / 6→IPv6) rồi protocol→port (cấp ephemeral port từ **49152**, chung TCP+UDP, chung 2 họ), **sau khi ráp lại gói phân mảnh** (IPv4 [`Ipv4Reassembler.Offer` @ :38](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4Reassembler.cs#L38) RFC 791 §3.2; IPv6 Fragment-header [`Ipv6Reassembler.Offer` @ :38](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv6Reassembler.cs#L38) RFC 8200 §4.5; cả 2 buffer theo (src,dst,id) + timeout + bound chống DoS). TCP active-open **FSM đầy đủ** (Closed/SynSent/Established/FinWait1/FinWait2/Closing/TimeWait/CloseWait/LastAck): MSS **suy từ link MTU** (`IPacketChannel.Mtu`−40, mặc định **1360**, clamp theo MSS peer quảng bá), **window scaling RFC 7323** (cửa sổ nhận hiệu lực ≈256 KB + scale cửa sổ peer khi negotiated), receive window field **65535**, ACK tích lũy, RST→IOException. **Phía gửi tin cậy** ([TrySendData @ :413](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L413)): retx queue + retransmit theo **RTO RFC 6298** ([OnRtoTimer @ :594](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L594), RTT SRTT/RTTVAR + ×2 backoff + give-up cap → fault) + **sliding-window flow control** (tôn trọng cửa sổ peer, [ProcessAck @ :438](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L438)) + **zero-window persist** ([OnPersistTimer @ :651](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L651)). **Phía nhận** reassembly out-of-order ([ReceiveData @ :304](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L304)); **half-close FSM đầy đủ** + TIME-WAIT linger ([AdvanceClose @ :370](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L370)); tunable [`TcpRetransmitOptions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpRetransmitOptions.cs); terminal (graceful CLOSED / RST / hết retry) → event `Closed` ⇒ stack gỡ khỏi `_connections` + dispose. **Congestion control NewReno** (cwnd/slow-start/fast-retransmit, RFC 5681/6582) trên nền flow control. **SACK (RFC 2018/6675)** đàm phán SACK-Permitted (cả 2 bên) → phía nhận sinh SACK blocks từ out-of-order, phía gửi retransmit **chọn lọc đúng hố** (`RetransmitHoles`) + pipe-fill `(_sndNxt−_sndUna)−sacked` (`InFlight`); không SACK → fallback NewReno. Tự tính checksum ([InternetChecksum.cs:6](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/InternetChecksum.cs#L6)). **Chiều gửi**: chokepoint [`SendIp` @ :156](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L156) tự **phân mảnh** datagram > `IPacketChannel.Mtu` ([`Ipv4.Fragment` @ :85](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Ipv4.cs#L85), RFC 791 §2.3, cắt trên ranh 8 byte) thay vì gửi nguyên với DF rồi bị drop — đối xứng reassembly inbound; MSS TCP suy từ link MTU (clamp theo MSS peer). **PMTUD động (RFC 1191/8201)**: segment TCP đi ra với cờ DF → router path nhỏ hơn trả **ICMP Fragmentation-Needed (type 3/code 4)** / **ICMPv6 Packet-Too-Big (type 2)**; [`TcpIpStack.DeliverPathMtu` @ :354](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L354) trích source-port+sequence của segment được quote → định tuyến về connection → [`TcpConnection.OnIcmpPacketTooBig` @ :333](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L333) **hạ MSS** (chỉ giảm, sàn 576/1280) + [`ResegmentRetxQueue` @ :694](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L694) chẻ retx queue in-flight thành mảnh vừa path + retransmit (phá black-hole). Chỉ TCP (UDP/ICMP không retx). **ICMP (RFC 792)** nay được xử lý: [`OnIcmp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs) tự trả lời Echo Request, [`PingAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs) gửi Echo Request + chờ Echo Reply (match identifier/sequence) → [`PingReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/PingReply.cs); Destination Unreachable trích đúng Echo Request đã gửi ⇒ [`IcmpUnreachableException`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IcmpUnreachableException.cs). Gói tới **local port không có socket** nay tự sinh phản hồi (cả 2 họ): TCP → **RST** ([`SendTcpReset` @ :368](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L368), RFC 793 p.36), UDP → **ICMP/ICMPv6 port-unreachable** ([`SendPortUnreachableV4` @ :404](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L404) / [`SendPortUnreachableV6` @ :416](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L416), RFC 1122 §3.2.2.1 / RFC 4443 §3.1). **Dual-stack**: TCP/UDP chạy y hệt trên IPv4 lẫn IPv6 — chỉ lớp IP bọc ([`IpLayer.Build`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/IpLayer.cs)) + pseudo-header checksum ([`InternetChecksum.PseudoHeaderSum`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/InternetChecksum.cs)) khác theo họ; ICMPv6 echo/dest-unreachable + Fragment-header reassembly + fragmentation. App-facing: [`SendAsync` @ :236](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Tcp/TcpConnection.cs#L236) (cạnh `Send` fire-and-forget) thêm **backpressure** (giới hạn buffer chưa-gửi theo `SendBufferHighWaterMark`) + **propagate fault** (`IOException` khi RST/give-up) cho `VpnNetworkStream` (P0.3). **Chưa** ND/SLAAC (point-to-point L3 không cần — thuộc tầng L2). |
| **Ethernet** *(L2.0–L2.9)* | [MacAddress.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MacAddress.cs#L9), [EthernetFrame.cs:8](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetFrame.cs#L8), [EthernetSwitch.cs:16](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.cs#L16) (+ [SwitchPort.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.SwitchPort.cs) base / [Port.cs:14](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.Port.cs#L14) host / [UplinkPort.cs](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.UplinkPort.cs) uplink), [VirtualHost.cs:23](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23), [ArpResolver.cs:26](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26), [NdiscResolver.cs:31](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/NdiscResolver.cs#L31), [DhcpV4Configurator.cs:30](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L30), [Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs:34](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs#L34), [EthernetAdapter.cs:24](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetAdapter.cs#L24), [MultiHostSession.cs:25](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MultiHostSession.cs#L25); slot [INeighborResolver.cs:12](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/INeighborResolver.cs#L12)/[IAddressConfigurator.cs:11](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IAddressConfigurator.cs#L11) | **Nền tầng L2**: (L2.0) codec khung Ethernet II 14 byte (`EthernetFrame.Build` + readers; EtherType IPv4 `0x0800`/IPv6 `0x86DD`/ARP `0x0806`) + `MacAddress` 48-bit (ulong-backed: parse/format, cờ broadcast/multicast/ipv6-mcast `33:33`, key FDB) — đối xứng codec `Ipv4`/`Ipv6`. (L2.1) **`EthernetSwitch`** học MAC in-memory: hai loại port dưới base `SwitchPort` — `ConnectHost(mac)→IEthernetChannel` (host `Port` switch sở hữu) và **`ConnectUplink(IEthernetChannel)→UplinkPortHandle`** (uplink port bọc kênh VPN ngoài: switch forward ra → `uplink.WriteFrameAsync`, `uplink.InboundFrame` → ingress vào switch — **đường gắn data-plane đa-host**, switch không sở hữu kênh). FDB `Dictionary<MacAddress,SwitchPort>` học src-MAC→port + forward (unicast-đã-học đi 1 port; broadcast/multicast/unknown-unicast **flood** port khác; không phản xạ ingress; MAC-move + disconnect purge FDB) — quyết định dưới lock, deliver ngoài lock (IEEE 802.1D §7, **không** STP/aging/VLAN/snooping). 2 **slot** `INeighborResolver` (ARP/NDISC) + `IAddressConfigurator` (trả `TunnelConfig`) khai báo ở Abstractions bằng **raw bytes/`IPAddress`** (tránh phụ thuộc vòng). (L2.2) **`VirtualHost`** = cầu nối L2↔L3 (`: IPacketChannel`): giữ MAC + port switch + resolver, **expose `IPacketChannel`** cho `TcpIpStack` — egress resolve dest-MAC qua `INeighborResolver` rồi wrap Ethernet → switch; ingress strip header → `InboundIpPacket` (khung non-IP/ARP → event `InboundNonIpFrame` seam cho L2.3); `Mtu=link−14` (kẹp MSS), `Medium=Ip`, resolve header L3 bằng offset cố định (không ref project IpStack — giữ no-horizontal-dep §2). (L2.3) **`ArpResolver`** hiện thực `INeighborResolver` IPv4 (RFC 826, codec `ArpPacket` 28 byte): egress resolve next-hop IP→MAC (cache + request/reply + timeout/retry + coalesce), học mọi gói ARP, **trả lời** request hỏi IP của ta; nhận khung ARP inbound qua seam `VirtualHost.InboundNonIpFrame`. (L2.4) **`NdiscResolver`** `INeighborResolver` IPv6 (RFC 4861, codec `Icmpv6Ndisc`, mirror ARP): NS-to-solicited-node/NA + học LLA + trả NA + **DAD** + **parse RA → `RouterAdvertisementInfo`** (gateway+prefix); ride trong IPv6 nên nối cả `InboundIpPacket` lẫn `InboundNonIpFrame`. (L2.5) **`DhcpV4Configurator`** `IAddressConfigurator` IPv4 (RFC 2131, codec `DhcpV4Packet`/`DhcpV4Options`): DISCOVER→OFFER→REQUEST→ACK qua broadcast UDP 68→67 → `TunnelConfig` (IP/prefix/route/DNS). (L2.6) **`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`** `IAddressConfigurator` IPv6 (RFC 4862 SLAAC + RFC 8415 DHCPv6, codec `Dhcpv6Packet`/`Dhcpv6Options` + helper `SlaacAddress`): chọn theo RA (do L2.4 parse) — **SLAAC** (prefix autonomous /64 → địa chỉ global EUI-64/opaque RFC 7217) + **DHCPv6 stateful** (cờ M/O/force → SOLICIT→ADVERTISE→REQUEST→REPLY qua UDP 546→547 tới `ff02::1:2`) → `TunnelConfig` v6 (`AssignedAddressV6`/prefix/route `::/0`/DNS); gửi RS tới `ff02::2` đợi RA. Tự dựng IPv4/IPv6+UDP + ICMPv6 (checksum pseudo-header RFC 768/791/8200) — **không** ref `IpStack`. (L2.7) **`EthernetAdapter`** ráp `EthernetSwitch` + N×`VirtualHost` + backpressure thành LAN userspace multi-host; `ConnectUplink(IEthernetChannel)` gắn uplink VPN vào switch như một port (data-plane đa-host). (L2.8) **`MultiHostSession`** phơi N station = N `EthernetHostSession` (`: IVpnSession`) trên adapter (mỗi station MAC/IP/`IPacketChannel`/`TunnelConfig` riêng, DHCP/SLAAC lease qua `AddStationAsync`) + năng lực driver tap/SoftEther khai báo `L2Ethernet`/`L2BroadcastDomain`/`SupportsMultiHost`. `ArpResolver.SetLocalAddress` cập nhật địa chỉ sau DHCP (station gắn trước khi lease). (L2.9) **composite dual-stack** `DualStackNeighborResolver` (route ARP/NDISC theo `AddressFamily`) + `DualStackAddressConfigurator` (merge DHCPv4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6 vào một `TunnelConfig`) để **một** host nói cả 2 họ — chốt tầng L2 với test multi-host dual-stack offline. **Cố ý lược bỏ**: VLAN 802.1Q/FCS/padding (codec); FDB aging/STP/snooping (switch); routing/gateway on-link; proxy/gratuitous ARP; NUD (NDISC); lease renew T1/T2 + DECLINE/RELEASE + Rapid-Commit/IA_PD + privacy-ext RFC 8981 (DHCPv6/SLAAC). **Data-plane đa-host đã có** (`ConnectUplink` + `MultiHostSession`); tiêu thụ bởi SoftEther + OpenVPN-tap (opt-in `multiHost`). |
| **Ipsec.Nat** | [NatTraversalChannel.cs:13](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversalChannel.cs#L13), [NatTraversal.cs:9](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversal.cs#L9) (enum [NatTPacketKind](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/Enums/NatTPacketKind.cs#L4), hằng `IkePort=500`/`NatTPort=4500`/`MarkerLength=4`) | NAT-T (RFC 3948): 1 UDP socket. **Bind local port ephemeral (≠500/4500)** để gateway coi client là NATed → **forced-NAT-T** (xem §8). [`SwitchToNatTPort()` @ :53](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversalChannel.cs#L53) (driver gọi sau khi IKE NAT-D phát hiện, không tự phát hiện) chuyển sang 4500; **ghép kênh IKE/ESP** trên 4500 (4 byte 0 ⇒ IKE; SPI≠0 ⇒ ESP). Trên port 500 phân loại bằng độ dài ≥28 (ISAKMP header), không marker. *(Gom từ project cũ `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Udp`; namespace `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec.Nat`.)* |

Vòng đời: keepalive **ping/ping-restart** (`OpenVpnKeepalive` + `OpenVpnPing.Magic`; drop ping inbound ở device-link) trong timer riêng (`StopAttemptLoop` dispose timer + tắt `_dataActive`), rekey = **re-establish** khi `OpenVpnDataPlane.RekeyNeeded` (~2³² packet-id, tránh tái dùng nonce GCM) gọi `OnLinkLost` của base, teardown (`DisconnectAsync` override gửi **explicit-exit-notify** `EXIT_NOTIFY` best-effort + time-box 2s trước `DisconnectCoreAsync`), supervisor/auto-reconnect (gom về base, không còn `_lifetimeCts`/`ReconnectLoopAsync`/`WithJitter`/`SetState` chép riêng). `OnReconnected` raise `Reconnected(OpenVpnReconnectInfo)`. **SỬA crash reconnect-window**: data-plane sink đọc `_transport` **hiện tại** + bỏ qua khi đang reconnect (`!_dataActive`) + nuốt `ObjectDisposedException`/`SocketException` ([sink @ OpenVpnConnection.cs:273](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/OpenVpnConnection.cs#L273)) — trước đây một RTO retransmit của TCP-stack bắn vào socket vừa dispose ⇒ unhandled trong timer ⇒ sập process; [`OpenVpnSocketTransportFactory.UdpDatagramSocket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenVpn/Transport/OpenVpnSocketTransportFactory.cs#L46) giữ ref `Socket` (tránh `UdpClient.Client` null khi dispose đua) + tắt `SIO_UDP_CONNRESET` trên Windows (ICMP port-unreachable không còn làm receive/send sau đó ném `ConnectionReset`). **Logging Q.2**: ctor nhận `ILoggerFactory?` (null⇒no-op) → handshake (reset/TLS/key-method-2/PUSH)/keepalive/rekey/state/link-lost/reconnect (test offline `OpenVpnLoggingTests.cs`). **Refs**: Abstractions + **Drivers.Core** + OpenVpn + Ethernet (fabric L2 cho tap). tun + tap-1-host: **1 IP ảo** (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`); **tap multi-host** (`multiHost: true`): N station = N `IVpnSession`, thêm qua `OpenSessionAsync`. tap IPv4/ARP (pure-DHCP đã có); **client-cert PEM auto-load + explicit-exit-notify + NCP-less fallback cipher (AEAD + AES-CBC non-AEAD) + P_DATA_V1/V2 đã có (V.2-occ)**; **IPv6 ifconfig cần NDISC L2.4**; soft-reset make-before-break là việc sau. **Validate live (đã chạy thật)**: tun/UDP tới VPN Gate (AES-128-CBC, NCP-less, P_DATA_V1) — tunnel lên + HTTP checkip (IP công cộng) + UDP DNS + ICMP 2 chiều;
