[`Pack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L17) = list [`PackElement`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackElement.cs#L12){`Name`≤63, [`PackValueType`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Enums/PackValueType.cs#L8) (`Int`=0/`Data`=1/`Str`=2/`UniStr`=3/`Int64`=4), mảng [`PackValue`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackValue.cs#L11) ≥1}; codec **big-endian** [`ToBytes`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L147)/[`Parse`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/Pack.cs#L160) thuần (**không I/O**) qua [`PackBufferWriter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferWriter.cs#L11)/[`PackBufferReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Pack/PackBufferReader.cs#L12): `uint32(num_elements)` → mỗi element `BufStr(name)·type·num_value·value[]`; **BufStr** prefix `len+1` không-NUL (quirk), **STR** prefix đúng-len Latin-1, **UNISTR** prefix `utf8len+1` + utf8 + **1 NUL**, INT/INT64 BE 4/8B, DATA `len`+bytes. Helper `Set*`/`Get*` theo tên (single + `Set*Array` đa-value) + tra cứu case-insensitive; input lỗi ⇒ `FormatException`. Test offline [`SoftEther.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther.Tests) (**25 test PACK**: round-trip mọi kiểu + đa-value array + tên dài 63 + bool + empty + case-insensitive + **byte-layout đối chiếu PACK dựng tay** (single-int/STR-no-+1/UNISTR-+1-trailing-NUL/INT64-BE) + **PACK hello/login mẫu** (hello/version/build/random + login với `secure_password`=SHA-0 qua `Sha0`) + reject underrun/đếm-vượt/trùng-tên).
- ✅ **SoftEther control handshake (V4.b)** — cùng project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther), **tách phần codec/state thuần khỏi I/O socket** (test offline qua server giả lập in-memory), nay **ref** [`Abstractions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions) (seam [`IByteStreamTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IByteStreamTransport.cs) F.1) + [`Crypto`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto) (SHA-0). Luồng [`SoftEtherHandshake.RunAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L177): (1) **watermark POST** [`SoftEtherWatermark.BuildRequest`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherWatermark.cs#L73) `POST /vpnsvc/connect.cgi HTTP/1.1` + headers + thân `signature‖padding` (signature là **placeholder byte-exact reproducible** [`DefaultSignature`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherWatermark.cs#L27) — **KHÔNG** copy blob GPL `Watermark.c`; server thật truyền blob qua `WithSignature`); (2) đọc hello PACK [`ParseHello`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L41) (`hello`/`version`/`build`/`random` 20B challenge); (3) dựng/gửi login PACK [`BuildLoginPack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L68) `method=login`/`hubname`/`username`/`authtype` + **`secure_password`** [`SoftEtherAuth.ComputeSecurePassword`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherAuth.cs#L76) = `SHA0(SHA0(password‖UPPER(username))‖random)` (tái dùng [`Sha0`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Sha0.cs) qua `IHashAlgo` — **password gốc không qua wire**) + session params (`max_connection`/`use_encrypt`/`use_compress`/`half_connection`/`unique_id`) ([`SoftEtherSessionParams`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherSessionParams.cs#L11)); (4) đọc welcome [`ParseWelcome`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L110) → `error`≠0 ⇒ [`SoftEtherProtocolException`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherProtocolException.cs#L9)(ErrorCode), else `session_name`/`session_key_32`. PACK đi trong thân HTTP qua [`SoftEtherHttpPackCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHttpPackCodec.cs#L15) (`uint32 len` + PACK; build POST/200 + parse). Test offline (**+17 test** `SoftEtherHandshakeTests.cs`).
- ✅ **SoftEther data plane Ethernet-over-TLS + driver L2 (V4.c)** — data plane ở project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther) (`DataChannel/`): codec block thuần [`SoftEtherDataFrameCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataFrameCodec.cs#L13) (`uint32(num_frames)` + mỗi frame `uint32(size)·bytes`, `EncodeBlock`/`EncodeSingle`/`DecodeBlock`/`IsKeepAlive`) + reader streaming [`SoftEtherDataBlockReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataBlockReader.cs#L16) (ráp 1 block qua partial read; EOF ranh block ⇒ rỗng) + [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) (`IEthernetChannel`: `WriteFrameAsync` encode block ra sink / `Deliver` raise `InboundFrame`, drop keep-alive). **Driver L2 thật đầu tiên** [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther) (V4.c) ráp end-to-end: TLS byte-stream ([`SoftEtherTlsTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/Transport/SoftEtherTlsTransport.cs#L18) sau seam [`ISoftEtherTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/Transport/ISoftEtherTransportFactory.cs#L13)) → `SoftEtherHandshake.RunAsync` (V4.b) → data session → **DHCP lease** [`DhcpV4Configurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L29) (SecureNAT) → bridge L2↔L3 [`ArpResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26) + [`VirtualHost`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23) → `IPacketChannel`; keep-alive + supervisor reconnect qua base [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<SoftEtherConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) dùng chung (F.6 — `EstablishAsync`/`CleanupAttemptResourcesAsync`/`StopAttemptLoop` dispose keep-alive timer + `OnReconnected` raise `Reconnected(SoftEtherReconnectInfo)`; `SoftEtherReconnectOptions : VpnReconnectOptions`). `VpnClientBuilder.UseSoftEther(hubName)`. **Multi-host opt-in** (`multiHost: true`): data channel gắn uplink-as-port vào `EthernetAdapter` + `MultiHostSession`, primary station + `OpenSessionAsync` thêm station (mỗi station DHCP lease riêng). **IPv6 trong tunnel opt-in `enableIpv6` (V.4-ipv6)**: ngoài ARP/DHCPv4, bridge dựng `NdiscResolver` (L2.4) + `Ipv6AddressConfigurator` (L2.6) qua `DualStackNeighborResolver`/`DualStackAddressConfigurator` (L2.9) trên cùng channel SecureNAT, link-local `fe80::/64`+EUI-64 (`SlaacAddress`), `ConfigureIpv6BestEffortAsync` chạy SLAAC/DHCPv6 đẩy `AssignedAddressV6`/`PrefixLengthV6` lên `TunnelConfig` — best-effort (server IPv4-only vẫn kết nối), mặc định tắt; cả 1-host lẫn multi-host (dual-stack station). `AssignedAddressV6`/`IsIpv6Enabled` + overload `UseSoftEther(hub, enableIpv6)`. Test offline (**+23 test**: `SoftEtherConnectionTests` end-to-end qua server SecureNAT giả lập — control + DHCP server + ARP responder + IP echo + 2 test multi-host + 3 test use_encrypt/use_compress + **3 test IPv6** (1-host SLAAC+DHCPv6-DNS+round-trip v4/v6 qua NDISC thật / IPv4-only-server vẫn Connected không-v6 / multi-host station v4+v6) — và `SoftEtherDataFrameCodecTests`). **Còn lại**: validate live (Q.1).
- ✅ **SoftEther multi-connection (V.4)** — 1–32 TCP/TLS song song = 1 session logic. Protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther)): [`ParseWelcome`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L110) nay đọc `max_connection` (server clamp theo policy hub) + `half_connection` → [`SoftEtherWelcomeInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherWelcomeInfo.cs#L9); codec [`BuildAdditionalConnectPack`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L140)/[`ParseAdditionalConnectReply`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L155) + driver I/O [`RunAdditionalConnectAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/SoftEtherHandshake.cs#L209) (watermark→hello→`method=additional_connect`+`session_name`(session key)→ack, server `GetSessionFromKey` gắn socket vào session đã login); [`SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux.cs#L26) gộp N transport thành 1 data path — egress block **round-robin** các connection gửi-được ([`SendBlockAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherMultiConnectionMux.cs#L97)), ingress **1 decode loop/connection** ([`SoftEtherDataBlockReader`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherDataBlockReader.cs#L16) reuse) gộp `InboundFrame` (frame self-contained ⇒ reassemble = hợp mọi connection, thứ tự trong-1-connection giữ nguyên), fault/peer-close ⇒ `linkLost` **một lần** (one-shot guard); [`SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherConnectionDirectionPlanner.cs#L19) chia hướng theo [`SoftEtherConnectionDirection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/Enums/SoftEtherConnectionDirection.cs#L9) (full-duplex ⇒ mọi `Both`; **half_connection** ⇒ nửa `Send`-only + nửa `Receive`-only, ≥1 mỗi hướng, 1 connection thì luôn `Both`). Driver [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther): sau login lấy `welcome.MaxConnection`, mở `min(login.MaxConnection, granted, 32)−1` connection phụ ([`OpenAdditionalConnectionsAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/SoftEtherConnection.cs)), gắn `SoftEtherEthernetChannel` lên mux (egress `mux.SendBlockAsync` + `mux.InboundFrame += channel.Deliver`), keep-alive đi qua mux; connection phụ fail = best-effort (log + chạy tiếp với số connection đã gắn); `ConnectionCount` phơi số connection. Test offline: protocol **+14 test** (`SoftEtherMultiConnectionTests` — codec additional_connect, welcome max/half, planner, mux round-robin/merge-ingress/half-duplex/link-lost-once) + driver **+4 test** (`SoftEtherMultiConnectionTests` qua `SoftEtherMultiConnectionServer` giả lập N-connection: 4-connection round-trip 40 gói không mất, clamp về số server cấp, single-connection vẫn chạy, half-duplex chia hướng vẫn 2 chiều). **Còn lại**: IPv6 tunnel, validate live (Q.1).
- ✅ **SoftEther payload codec use_compress/use_encrypt (V.4)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther), `DataChannel/`). **use_compress**: [`SoftEtherPayloadCompressor`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherPayloadCompressor.cs#L23) nén **per-frame** bằng DEFLATE (`System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream`, RFC 1951, cả 2 TFM) **trước** khi block-encode; frame nén mang prefix magic `0xDEADBEEFCAFEFACE` (doc [`07`](07-softether.md) §"Multi-host & multi-connection") + chỉ gửi nén khi nhỏ hơn (frame không nén được giữ thô → receiver phân biệt qua magic); giải nén ở [`DecompressFrame`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherPayloadCompressor.cs#L55) (inflate vượt `MaxFrameSize`/stream hỏng ⇒ `FormatException`). Hook vào [`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEthernetChannel.cs#L19) qua cờ ctor `useCompress` (`WriteFrameAsync` nén / `Deliver` giải-nén) — codec block + reader **giữ nguyên**. **use_encrypt**: [`SoftEtherEncryptedTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L22) decorator `IByteStreamTransport` áp RC4 keystream **liên tục per-direction** (dưới block framing — đúng behavior SoftEther, RC4 nằm dưới framing), **tái dùng** [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs) (F.5b); 2 keystream độc lập (RC4 order-sensitive) suy từ session key + nhãn hướng 1 byte qua [`DeriveDirectionKeys`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/DataChannel/SoftEtherEncryptedTransport.cs#L61) (`CreateClient`/`CreateServer` mirror nhau). Thứ tự egress **compress-rồi-encrypt** (ciphertext không nén được). Driver [`Drivers.SoftEther`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther) wire theo `login.Session.UseCompress`/`UseEncrypt` (RC4 bọc connection sau handshake plaintext, dùng `welcome.SessionKey`). **Mặc định tắt** ([`SoftEtherSessionParams.UseEncrypt`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.SoftEther/Models/SoftEtherSessionParams.cs#L24)/`UseCompress` mặc định `false`) — payload thô trên TLS, không vỡ test cũ; RC4 broken (RFC 7465) chỉ để interop legacy trên TLS. Test offline: protocol **+9 test** (`SoftEtherPayloadCodecTests` — compressor nén/raw-passthrough/corrupt + RC4 mirror 2 chiều/ciphertext≠plaintext + block round-trip 4 tổ hợp) + driver **+3 test** (`SoftEtherConnectionTests.Connect_WithEncryptAndCompress_RoundTripsIp` end-to-end qua server giả lập mirror RC4+DEFLATE). **Còn lại**: validate live (Q.1) — watermark/PACK/SecureNAT thật.
- ✅ Enum năng lực **SoftEther** (driver) nay có hiện thực (`VpnLinkLayer.L2Ethernet` + `SecurityKind.Tls` + `AuthMethod.UserPassword` + `AddressAssignment.Dhcp` + `MultiHostModel.L2BroadcastDomain`). **DTLS** vẫn là **khung mở rộng**, chưa hiện thực. Hợp đồng L2 [IEthernetChannel](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IEthernetChannel.cs#L7) nay có impl src (`EthernetSwitch.Port` + `OpenVpnTapChannel` + **`SoftEtherEthernetChannel`**) + nền L2 (codec + switch học MAC + `VirtualHost` bridge L2↔L3 + **ARP IPv4** `ArpResolver` + **NDISC IPv6** `NdiscResolver` (NS/NA/DAD/RA-parse) + **DHCPv4** `DhcpV4Configurator` (DISCOVER/OFFER/REQUEST/ACK→`TunnelConfig`), L2.0–L2.5) đã có; **driver L2 thật (SoftEther + OpenVPN-tap) tiêu thụ end-to-end** cả **1-host** lẫn **multi-host data-plane** (uplink-as-port `ConnectUplink` + `MultiHostSession`); nền L2 nay đầy đủ (SLAAC/DHCPv6 L2.6 + `EthernetAdapter` L2.7 + `MultiHostSession` L2.8 + composite dual-stack L2.9 + uplink-as-port).
- ✅ **OpenConnect/AnyConnect codec (V5.a)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang WireGuard/SoftEther; chỉ ref `Abstractions`): **CSTP framing 8-byte** [`CstpFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpFraming.cs#L19) (header `STF·0x01·length(2 BE)·type·0x00`, `Encode`/`Decode` + reassembler `Append`/`TryReadPacket` qua mọi ranh đọc TLS, magic hỏng ⇒ `FormatException`; [`CstpPacketType`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Enums/CstpPacketType.cs#L9) DATA/DPD-REQ/DPD-RESP/DISCONNECT/KEEPALIVE/COMPRESSED/TERMINATE — hiện thực OpenConnect của **seam F.2 `IPacketEncapsulator`**); **HTTP auth ocserv** [`OpenConnectAuthCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectAuthCodec.cs#L14) (XML `<config-auth>` init/auth-reply + parse `<form><input/>` → [`OpenConnectAuthForm`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Models/OpenConnectAuthForm.cs#L11) + `IsSuccess` + `ExtractCookie` `webvpn=`); **HTTP CONNECT** [`OpenConnectConnectCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnectCodec.cs#L17) (`CONNECT /CSCOSSLC/tunnel` + parse `X-CSTP-*` → [`OpenConnectTunnelInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Models/OpenConnectTunnelInfo.cs#L14) → `TunnelConfig`, non-200 ⇒ `UnauthorizedAccessException`). **Pure codec, không I/O** (re-implement từ draft-mavrogiannopoulos-openconnect + ocserv, **không copy GPL**).
- ✅ **OpenConnect data plane + driver (V5.b, TLS-only)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): [`CstpChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpChannel.cs#L24) = `IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-TLS bọc `IByteStreamTransport`+`CstpFraming` (DATA framing/demux + DPD-REQ→event reply + DISCONNECT/TERMINATE→`PeerClosed` + event `PacketSent`/`PacketReceived` bơm timer); [`OpenConnectHttpTransactor`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectHttpTransactor.cs#L18) chạy auth POST + CONNECT **byte-exact** (header tới CRLFCRLF rồi đúng `Content-Length`, **không nuốt** gói CSTP đầu sau CONNECT 200); [`CstpDpdState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDpdState.cs#L17) DPD/keepalive **clock-inject** (`ShouldSendDpd`/`IsPeerDead` theo `X-CSTP-DPD` dead-window 2× + `ShouldSendKeepalive` theo `X-CSTP-Keepalive`, như `OpenVpnKeepalive`/`WireGuardPeerState`). Driver [`Drivers.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect): TLS byte-stream ([`OpenConnectSocketTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/Transport/OpenConnectSocketTransportFactory.cs#L24) inline cùng shape SSTP `TlsByteStream` F.1, sau seam [`IOpenConnectTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/Transport/IOpenConnectTransportFactory.cs#L12)) → auth (username/password từ `VpnCredentials`) → CONNECT → bind `CstpChannel` qua `SwappablePacketChannel` + receive loop + DPD/keepalive timer; DISCONNECT/TERMINATE/dead → teardown + supervisor/auto-reconnect (mirror WireGuard/OpenVPN/SoftEther); `VpnClientBuilder.UseOpenConnect`. **1 IP ảo** (`OpenSessionAsync`⇒`NotSupported`), **không PPP** (in-band X-CSTP-*). **DTLS data path nay đã wire (V5.c — bullet dưới)** + **rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-* nay đã wire (V5.d — bullet dưới)**; **dialect Fortinet/F5/GlobalProtect** + **validate live ocserv (Q.1)** là việc sau.
- ✅ **DTLS 1.2 datagram transport (F.3)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls) (tầng TRANSPORT, ngang `TlsByteStream` F.1; chỉ ref `Abstractions` + PackageReference `BouncyCastle.Cryptography` 2.4.0 **không điều kiện cả 2 TFM**): concrete [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L9) qua **BouncyCastle** (`Org.BouncyCastle.Tls.DtlsClientProtocol`) — `SslStream` BCL **không** làm DTLS trên `net8.0` lẫn `netstandard2.0`. [`DtlsDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28) bọc một inner `IDatagramTransport` (UDP plaintext): `ConnectAsync` chạy handshake DTLS 1.2 client (pin `ProtocolVersion.DTLSv12`, chào AEAD ECDHE/DHE-RSA+ECDSA+RSA-KT AES-GCM ở [`DefaultDtlsClient`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DefaultDtlsClient.cs#L15)) rồi `SendAsync`/`ReceiveAsync` = 1 DTLS record mã hóa/giải mã (giữ ranh giới datagram — drop-in thay UDP thô), phơi `SendLimit`/`ReceiveLimit`, `DisposeAsync` gửi close_notify. Cert server validate/pin qua tùy chọn [`DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsServerCertificateValidationCallback.cs#L15) (null⇒accept all; reject⇒`TlsFatalAlert`); client **anonymous**. Record layer BouncyCastle **đồng bộ** → cầu sync↔async [`BouncyCastleDatagramBridge`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/BouncyCastleDatagramBridge.cs#L19) (vòng nền pull inbound vào `BlockingCollection`; `Receive(...,waitMillis)` timeout⇒`-1` cho retransmit timer DTLS; `Send` đồng bộ), handshake + mỗi send/receive offload `Task.Run`, chịu **1 sender + 1 receiver** đồng thời. **Consumer:** OpenConnect V5.c (đã wire — bullet dưới). Test offline (**+7 test** [`Transport.Dtls.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls.Tests)) dựng **server DTLS giả lập** (`DtlsServerProtocol` + cert RSA self-signed) qua loopback datagram in-memory: handshake xong, round-trip 2 chiều nhiều datagram, cert-callback quan sát đúng cert server, reject-cert ⇒ abort handshake, **record loss** (drop flight đầu ⇒ DTLS retransmit ⇒ vẫn xong) + **reorder** (đảo 2 datagram đầu server ⇒ vẫn xong). **Chỉ DTLS 1.2** (DTLS 1.3 chưa chào); validate live (Q.1) chờ.
- ✅ **OpenConnect DTLS data path song song + fallback TLS (V5.c)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): [`CstpDatagramFraming`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDatagramFraming.cs#L13) (framing CSTP cho DTLS = header **1-byte type**, **không** STF magic/length — 1 datagram = 1 gói, `Encode`/`Decode`, đối xứng `CstpFraming` 8-byte của đường TLS) + [`CstpDatagramChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpDatagramChannel.cs#L19) (`IPacketChannel` CSTP-over-DTLS bọc `IDatagramTransport`+`CstpDatagramFraming`: `WriteIpPacketAsync` đóng khung DATA, `RunReceiveLoopAsync` đọc datagram→demux DATA/DPD/DISCONNECT, raise **cùng event** `DpdRequestReceived`/`PeerClosed`/`PacketReceived`/`PacketSent` như `CstpChannel` để dùng chung `CstpDpdState`). Parse thêm **X-DTLS-*** vào [`OpenConnectTunnelInfo`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Models/OpenConnectTunnelInfo.cs#L14) (`DtlsSessionId`/`DtlsCipherSuite`/`DtlsPort`/`DtlsKeepalive`/`DtlsDpd` + `HasDtls`) ở [`OpenConnectConnectCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnectCodec.cs#L17) + advertise DTLS trong CONNECT request (`requestDtls`→`X-DTLS-Master-Secret`+`X-DTLS-CipherSuite`). Driver [`Drivers.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect) (ref thêm [`Transport.Dtls`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls) F.3): seam UDP [`IOpenConnectDatagramTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/Transport/IOpenConnectDatagramTransportFactory.cs#L15) (production [`OpenConnectSocketDatagramTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/Transport/OpenConnectSocketDatagramTransportFactory.cs#L19) socket UDP thật, test loopback). [`OpenConnectConnection.TryEstablishDtlsAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnection.cs#L281): sau CONNECT, nếu server đẩy `X-DTLS-*` (`HasDtls`) + có datagram factory ⇒ mở UDP tới `X-DTLS-Port` → bọc [`DtlsDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Dtls/DtlsDatagramTransport.cs#L28) (session-id = cookie tương quan) → handshake DTLS 1.2 (bound timeout, mặc định 10s) → swap data plane sang `CstpDatagramChannel` qua `SwappablePacketChannel` (kênh CSTP-over-TLS giữ làm control/fallback), DPD/keepalive bơm trên kênh active. **Fallback TLS** khi: không đẩy `X-DTLS-*`, không có factory, hoặc handshake DTLS fail/timeout (giữ nguyên kênh TLS đã bind, không vỡ connect). `OpenConnectDriver` mặc định `enableDtls=true` (capabilities `Tls|Dtls`); cap về `Tls` khi `enableDtls=false`. Test offline (**+4 test** `Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests`: DTLS data path end-to-end qua server DTLS giả lập BouncyCastle (`SimulatedDtlsCstpServer` — `DtlsServerProtocol`+cert self-signed, decode 1-byte CSTP, echo DATA/đáp DPD) trên loopback UDP — IP round-trip 2 chiều + `IsDtlsDataPlane`, DPD server-probe đáp qua DTLS, **fallback khi X-DTLS-* không có**, **fallback khi handshake DTLS fail**; **+5 test codec** `OpenConnect.Tests`: `CstpDatagramFraming` round-trip + reject empty, parse X-DTLS-*/`HasDtls`, advertise DTLS trong CONNECT request). **Còn lại**: tương quan session-id qua **DTLS ClientHello session_id** thật + interop AnyConnect/ocserv (lab Q.1).
- ✅ **OpenConnect rekey X-CSTP-Rekey-Method (V5.d)** — protocol-level (project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect)): enum [`OpenConnectRekeyMethod`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/Enums/OpenConnectRekeyMethod.cs#L9) (None/Ssl/NewTunnel) + `OpenConnectTunnelInfo.ParsedRekeyMethod` (parse `X-CSTP-Rekey-Method`, None khi `none`/unknown/`X-CSTP-Rekey-Time`≤0) + [`CstpRekeyState`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect/CstpRekeyState.cs#L18) timer **clock-inject** (`ShouldRekey`/`OnRekeyDone` theo `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time`, cùng shape `CstpDpdState`). Driver [`Drivers.OpenConnect`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect): `OpenConnectConnection` (`partial`) arm `CstpRekeyState` ở `EstablishAsync`; timer loop `TimerTickAsync` `ShouldRekey` ⇒ [`RekeyAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect/OpenConnectConnection.cs#L517) **re-establish make-before-break**: `BuildCstpChannelAsync` (helper không-chạm-field) dựng tunnel mới (auth + CONNECT + `CstpChannel` + tùy chọn DTLS) vào biến cục bộ **trong khi** tunnel cũ vẫn chở traffic, rồi swap `Facade.SetInner` + field + token receive-loop mới (`_recvCts` rotate, cancel được loop cũ độc lập), cuối mới tear-down tunnel cũ (detach event ⇒ EOF cũ không gọi `OnLinkLost` → DISCONNECT → cancel/await loop cũ → dispose). `RekeyCount`/`Rekeyed`; guard `_rekeyInProgress` chống chạy chồng (và không bao giờ overlap reconnect). **Cả `new-tunnel` lẫn `ssl` đều re-establish**: `SslStream` net8/ns2.0 **không** lộ TLS-renegotiation phía client (chỉ net9+ `ExportKeyingMaterial`/renegotiate) ⇒ `ssl` là fallback re-establish (ghi chú ở `OpenConnectRekeyMethod`). Rekey lỗi (`MaybeRekeyAsync` catch) ⇒ **giữ tunnel hiện tại** + re-arm; DPD/keepalive + supervisor lo session chết thật. IP stack không re-bind ⇒ tunnel **không rớt** khi rekey. **Còn lại**: kiểm chứng **live** ocserv đặt `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time` ngắn (lab Q.1). Test offline (**+3 test** [`Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests/OpenConnectRekeyTests.cs) + harness `MultiAttemptOpenConnectFactory` dựng server mới mỗi connect, clock-inject): rekey kích hoạt đúng `X-CSTP-Rekey-Time` (`new-tunnel`) ⇒ re-establish (attempts≥2) + swap sang tunnel mới (đổi địa chỉ `10.10.0.9`) + round-trip qua tunnel mới + state vẫn `Connected`; `ssl` cũng re-establish; **không advertise Rekey-Time ⇒ không rekey** (RekeyCount=0); **+4 test** [`OpenConnect.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.OpenConnect.Tests/CstpRekeyStateTests.cs) (`CstpRekeyStateTests` — `ParsedRekeyMethod` map method/period (theory), `ShouldRekey` đúng-sau-period + `OnRekeyDone` re-arm + None-method disabled; +1 assert `ParsedRekeyMethod=Ssl` ở `OpenConnectConnectCodecTests`).
- ✅ **MPPE + RC4 crypto legacy (F.5b — nền PPTP V.6)** — trong project [`Crypto`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto): [`Rc4`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Rc4.cs#L13) (stream cipher KSA/PRGA, `Process`/`GenerateKeystream`/`Apply`) + [`MppeKeyDerivation`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeKeyDerivation.cs#L18) (RFC 3078 §7.3 `GetNewKeyFromSha` = `SHA1(StartKey‖40×0x00‖SessionKey‖40×0xF2)`, **initial key SHA-only** RFC 3079 §3.1 + **re-key SHA→`RC4(InterimKey, InterimKey)`** RFC 3078, strength reduction 40→`0xD1 0x26 0x9E`/56→`0xD1`/128 nguyên) + [`MppeSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16) (1 chiều: RC4 state + coherency count 12-bit + framing header A(flush)/B/C/D(encrypt) RFC 3078 §3.1, `Encrypt`/`Decrypt`; **stateless** = re-key + FLUSHED mỗi gói, **stateful** = re-key mỗi 256 gói khi low-octet coherency=0xFF). MPPE start key suy từ MS-CHAPv2 qua [`MsChapV2.DeriveMppeMasterKey`/`DeriveMppeSendStartKey`/`DeriveMppeReceiveStartKey`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/MsChapV2.cs#L156) — **tái dùng `GetMasterKey`/`GetAsymmetricStartKey` sẵn có**, thêm cờ `isServer` chọn Magic2/Magic3 (client-send=server-receive=Magic2; client-receive=server-send=Magic3). **CẢNH BÁO BẢO MẬT: MPPE + MS-CHAPv2 đã bị phá hoàn toàn** (RC4 RFC 7465, MS-CHAPv2 brute-force DES) — chỉ tương thích PPTP legacy. **Chưa wire driver** (CCP negotiator + GRE data plane ở V.6.a). KAT offline: RC4 RFC 6229 (40/128-bit keystream) + classic Rivest; MPPE RFC 3079 §3.5 (MasterKey `FDECE371…`/StartKey `8B7CDC14…`/SessionKey 40/56/128) + "Sample Encrypted Message" `rc4(SessionKey,"test message")` (byte cuối 56-bit §3.5.2 là erratum RFC, giá trị thật `…57B8`); session round-trip stateless/stateful qua 600 gói.
- ✅ **PPTP control plane + CCP/MPPE negotiate (V6.a, offline)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp) (PROTOCOL-layer, ngang OpenConnect/WireGuard; ref `Abstractions`+`Crypto`+`Ppp`): **control codec TCP/1723** [`PptpControlCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlCodec.cs#L22) (header chung 12-byte `Length·MsgType·MagicCookie 0x1A2B3C4D·CtrlMsgType·Reserved0` + body big-endian/ASCII NUL-pad cho mọi message RFC 2637 §2.x: SCCRQ/SCCRP/OCRQ/OCRP/Echo/Set-Link-Info/Call-Clear/CDN/Stop-CC; `Encode`/`Decode` + reassembler `Append`/`TryReadMessage` qua mọi ranh đọc TCP, magic/length sai ⇒ `FormatException`); **state machine** [`PptpControlConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/PptpControlConnection.cs#L22) (PNS/client trên `IByteStreamTransport`: SCCRQ→SCCRP → OCRQ→OCRP ghi `PeerCallId`=GRE Call-ID → Echo keep-alive (auto-reply) + Set-Link-Info → Call-Clear→CDN + Stop-CC; refuse ⇒ `InvalidOperationException`); **CCP/MPPE** [`CcpNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/CcpNegotiator.cs#L22) **kế thừa [`PppNegotiator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppNegotiator.cs#L11) dùng chung** (RFC 1962): offer option MPPE đơn (RFC 2118/3078 type 18), `OnNak` adopt + `EvaluatePeerRequest` cap về cường độ tối đa + pin 1 bit, `OnReject`⇒`NotSupportedException`; [`MppeConfigOption`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeConfigOption.cs#L19) codec 4-byte supported-bits ↔ [`MppeKeyStrength`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/Enums/MppeKeyStrength.cs)/stateless; [`MppeSessionFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs#L20) ráp cặp [`MppeSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto/Mppe/MppeSession.cs#L16) (F.5b) từ MS-CHAPv2 (`DeriveMppeMasterKey`/asymmetric Send-Receive start key RFC 3079) + kết quả CCP. **Thêm `PppProtocol.Ccp`=0x80FD/`Compressed`=0x00FD** ở Ppp. **MS-CHAPv2+MPPE/RC4 đã bị phá — chỉ tương thích legacy.** Test offline (**+31 test** `Pptp.Tests`): codec round-trip mọi control message + đúng kích thước wire (156/168/32/16/20/24/148B) + reject magic/length sai + reassembler split-5-byte qua 3 gói; state machine end-to-end qua PAC giả lập (establish→call→echo→clear→stop) + refuse-control/refuse-call; CCP negotiate 128-bit/Nak-down-to-40 + multi-bit→Nak-strongest + unknown-option→reject + reject-MPPE→`NotSupportedException`; `MppeConfigOption` codec BE + strength→bit; `MppeSessionFactory` interop encrypt/decrypt 2 chiều 40/56/128-bit + stateless 5 gói.
- ✅ **PPTP GRE + MPPE data plane (V6.b, offline)** — bổ sung [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp): **GRE codec** [`PptpGreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreCodec.cs#L21)/[`PptpGrePacket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGrePacket.cs#L11) (Enhanced GRE RFC 2637 §4.1: version 1, Key high word=payload length/low word=Call ID, Sequence/Acknowledgment tùy chọn — codec thuần Encode/TryDecode) + **kênh data plane** [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) (`IPppFrameChannel` trên `IDatagramTransport` proto-47: lọc theo `localCallId`, sequence tăng + ack piggyback §4.4, receive-loop identity-guard + dispose-to-unblock kiểu native-ESP, strip/re-prepend HDLC `FF 03`) + **decorator MPPE** [`MppePppFrameChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppePppFrameChannel.cs#L23) (chạy CCP nội bộ giữa `PppEngine` ↔ GRE; LCP plaintext, còn lại mã hóa `MppeSession` thành proto 0x00FD khi CCP Opened). **OFFLINE only — driver runtime + validate live chờ F.9 raw-IP** (elevate). Test offline (`Pptp.Tests`): GRE codec round-trip plain/+seq/+ack + reject wrong-version/magic; channel cặp 2 đầu qua loopback `IDatagramTransport` trao đổi PPP frame + drop wrong-Call-ID + sequence/ack piggyback; MPPE decorator CCP-opened encrypt↔decrypt.
- ✅ **PPTP driver runtime (V6.b, offline)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp) (DRIVER-layer; ref `Abstractions`+`Drivers.Core`+`Ppp`+`Pptp`): [`PptpConnection`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/PptpConnection.cs) **kế thừa** [`ReconnectingVpnConnection<PptpConnectionState>`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Core/ReconnectingVpnConnection.cs#L24) — `EstablishAsync`: control TCP/1723 (seam [`PptpControlTransportFactory`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/PptpControlTransportFactory.cs), default real [`PptpControlTcpTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/Transport/PptpControlTcpTransport.cs)) → OCRQ/OCRP lấy Call-IDs → GRE proto-47 qua `IRawIpTransportFactory` → [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) → [`MppePppFrameChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppePppFrameChannel.cs#L23) → [`PppEngine`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/PppEngine.cs) [`MsChapV2Authenticator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ppp/Auth/MsChapV2Authenticator.cs) **tái dùng nguyên** (AuthSucceeded→StartCcp; chờ CCP-opened+IPCP-LinkUp trong HandshakeTimeout; AuthFailed⇒`VpnAuthenticationException`, timeout⇒`VpnNetworkTimeoutException`) → bind `Facade` + Echo-Request keepalive; `CleanupAttemptResourcesAsync` null-rồi-dispose GRE + Call-Clear/Stop-CC time-box 2s (gate theo control-state) mirror cleanup L2TP. [`PptpDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Pptp/PptpDriver.cs) (`IVpnProtocolDriver` Name=`pptp`, Caps Tcp+RawIp/Mppe/UserPassword/RequiresElevation) + [`VpnClientBuilder.UsePptp`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient/VpnClientBuilder.cs). **Thêm [`MppeSessionFactory.CreateServerSessions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Ccp/MppeSessionFactory.cs)** (đối xứng `CreateClientSessions`, RFC 3079 `isServer:true`) cho vai server/test. **OFFLINE code+test; validate live (poptop/accel-ppp Docker, elevate) chờ Q.1. MS-CHAPv2+MPPE/RC4 đã bị phá — chỉ tương thích legacy.** Test offline (**+5 test** `Drivers.Pptp.Tests`, không socket thật): control handshake qua PAC giả lập sinh đúng Local/Peer Call-ID; client GRE-wrap LCP Configure-Request đầu tiên với `PeerCallId` tới được server-end (decode `PptpGreCodec`); frame server→client tới được kênh GRE client; khóa MPPE client↔server round-trip 2 chiều (`CreateClientSessions`/`CreateServerSessions`); refuse control-connection ⇒ connect fail; caps driver. **Defer Q.1**: MS-CHAPv2 server-auth đầy đủ + CCP/MPPE Opened end-to-end + IPCP→`Connected` (lib chưa có server-side PPP MS-CHAPv2).
- ✅ **IP-in-IP / GRE thuần OFFLINE (V.8 phase a — code + test offline)** — project mới [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap) (PROTOCOL-layer; ref **chỉ Abstractions**): ba kiểu encapsulation **TRẦN không mã hóa** chở gói IP thẳng trên proto-number riêng qua một [`IDatagramTransport`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Transport/Interfaces/IDatagramTransport.cs#L10) raw-IP (F.9), mỗi kiểu một [`IPacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IPacketChannel.cs#L6) (L3, MaxHeaderLength=0). **GRE chuẩn v0** (RFC 2784 base + RFC 2890 Key/Seq + checksum RFC 1071): [`GrePacket`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/Gre/GrePacket.cs#L14)/[`GreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/Gre/GreCodec.cs#L24) (`Encode`/`TryDecode`; header byte0 `C R0 K S s Recur(3)`, byte1 `Reserved0(5) Version(3)`=0, ProtocolType(2); thứ tự field tùy chọn **Checksum(2)+Reserved1(2) → Key(4) → Sequence(4)**; validate Version==0/bounds/checksum-zero, **leniency** bỏ qua Reserved0/routing/recursion) + [`GreTunnelChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/Gre/GreTunnelChannel.cs#L22) (ctor `(IDatagramTransport, GreTunnelOptions?, ILogger?)`; outbound chọn proto-type `0x0800`/`0x86DD` theo version nibble + stamp Key/Seq/Checksum theo [`GreTunnelOptions`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/Gre/GreTunnelOptions.cs#L9); receive-loop `TryDecode` drop non-GRE/malformed/proto-type-lạ → raise `InboundIpPacket`; `Start()` + identity-guard + dispose-to-unblock như [`PptpGreChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreChannel.cs#L21) / native-ESP loop). **KHÁC PPTP Enhanced GRE** (v1, key=payload-len+call-id) — codec riêng **không** tái dùng [`PptpGreCodec`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Pptp/Gre/PptpGreCodec.cs#L21). **IPIP** (proto-4, RFC 2003 — IPv4-in-IPv4) + **SIT/6in4** (proto-41, RFC 4213 — IPv6-in-IPv4): **một** [`RawIpPassthroughChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap/RawIpPassthroughChannel.cs#L21) header-less dùng chung (outbound gửi gói IP verbatim làm datagram; inbound raise payload verbatim; family-agnostic — proto-number do caller chọn lúc tạo transport). Thêm hằng [`RawIpProtocols.IpIp=4`/`.Sit=41`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.RawIp/RawIpProtocols.cs#L4) cho caller (kênh **không** ref Transport.RawIp). **Refs**: chỉ Abstractions (`ILogger`/`NullLogger` qua transitive). **OFFLINE codec+kênh+test; driver (b) + EtherIP(proto-97)/L2TPv3(proto-115) + validate live (c, cần IP public) chờ Q.1.** ⚠️ TRẦN không mã hóa — chỉ mạng tin cậy hoặc kèm IPsec ESP. Test offline (**+14 test** [`IpEncap.Tests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests), không socket thật): [`GreCodecTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/GreCodecTests.cs) (round-trip plain/+Key/+Seq/+Checksum/combined + thứ tự byte chính xác + v4/v6 proto-type + malformed version≠0/truncated/bad-checksum + leniency Reserved0), [`GreTunnelChannelTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/GreTunnelChannelTests.cs) (cặp kênh qua loopback `IDatagramTransport`: inner v4/v6 round-trip **byte-for-byte** + garbage dropped), [`RawIpPassthroughChannelTests`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpEncap.Tests/RawIpPassthroughChannelTests.cs) (v4/v6 verbatim). Build xanh cả `netstandard2.0` + `net8.0`.

- ✅ **Audit cancellation/timeout & thread-safety (Q.3)** — soát toàn bộ receive-loop / channel / `CancellationToken` xuyên solution (driver `*Connection`, [`SwappablePacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/SwappablePacketChannel.cs#L14), transport receive-loop, IpStack loop). **1 lỗi material đã sửa**: [`UdpConnection.ReceiveAsync`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/Udp/UdpConnection.cs#L45) đăng ký callback hủy theo **field `_waiter`** thay vì **local waiter** — một datagram tới trên thread khác null-out field (và complete chính TCS đó) **trước** khi `cancellationToken.Register(...)` chạy, callback nhận `null` ⇒ NRE trên thread hủy (đồng bộ, ngay trong `ReceiveAsync` nếu token đã hủy sẵn; hoặc văng ra từ `CancellationTokenSource.Cancel()`). Sửa: capture TCS vào local rồi `Register` theo local (đúng pattern [`TcpIpStack.PingAsync` @ :107](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs#L107)) — **không đổi hành vi happy-path**. Phần còn lại (receive-loop driver honor token + route fault qua `OnLinkLost`, [`BackpressuredPacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/BackpressuredPacketChannel.cs#L24) single-reader + cancel sạch, [`SwappablePacketChannel`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/SwappablePacketChannel.cs#L14) swap dưới lock + write lock-free volatile, `_random` serialise, ConfigureAwait(false) phủ khắp lib cho consumer ns2.0) **không có lỗi material** — chốt invariant bằng test concurrency. Test offline (**+4 test** IpStack.Tests): [`UdpConnectionCancellationTests.cs`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack.Tests/UdpConnectionCancellationTests.cs) (honor-cancel khi không có datagram, token-hủy-sẵn ⇒ `OperationCanceledException` không NRE, **stress 200 vòng delivery↔cancel đua nhau** không NRE/treo) + [`SwappablePacketChannelTests.Facade_ConcurrentSwapsAndWrites_*`](../tests/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack.Tests/SwappablePacketChannelTests.cs) (swap+write+inbound đồng thời không vỡ + quiesce trên inner cuối ⇒ forward đúng exactly-one-subscriber).

`InitiateHandshake` rồi im khi handshake đang bay, **rekey tại t=120s** (`NeedsRekey`/`Evaluate`=InitiateHandshake, chưa dead) + **phiên chết t≥180s** (`IsSessionDead`), rekey/reject theo đếm gói (giới hạn nhỏ inject), **resend mỗi REKEY_TIMEOUT 5s** + tôn trọng jitter inject, **bỏ cuộc sau REKEY_ATTEMPT_TIME 90s** (`AbandonHandshake`, resend nhường abandon, `Reset` về cold), **gói IP round-trip trong khung Ethernet** nổi lên facade L3 + ping (magic trần) bị drop; (2) **pure-DHCP** — PUSH_REPLY không-ifconfig + server chạy DHCP behind bridge ⇒ `DhcpV4Configurator` lease + malformed status ⇒ `FormatException` + require host/cookie), **+6 test driver OpenConnect (V5.b, Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests)** (`OpenConnectConnectionTests.cs` + harness **+DPD client-probe** (clock-inject qua `X-CSTP-DPD` 2s im lặng) ⇒ client gửi DPD-REQUEST, server đáp giữ tunnel up; **+DISCONNECT từ server** (reconnect tắt) ⇒ teardown về Disconnected; **+driver** `OpenConnectDriver` cap L3Ip/Tls/Tls/ConfigPush/no-PPP + `ConnectAsync` phơi 1 session + data qua facade + `OpenSessionAsync` ⇒ `NotSupported`; server là test harness không có server product), **+4 test DTLS data path OpenConnect (V5.c, Drivers.OpenConnect.Tests)** (`OpenConnectConnectionTests.cs` + harness `LoopbackDatagramLink.cs`/`SimulatedDtlsCstpServer.cs` — server DTLS giả lập BouncyCastle trên loopback UDP: data plane swap sang DTLS (`IsDtlsDataPlane`) + **IP round-trip 2 chiều CSTP-over-DTLS** + DPD server-probe đáp qua DTLS, **fallback CSTP-over-TLS khi X-DTLS-* không advertise**, **fallback khi DTLS handshake fail/timeout** — connect không vỡ; cap DTLS mặc định `Tls|Dtls`) + **+5 test codec DTLS OpenConnect (V5.c, OpenConnect.Tests)** (`CstpDatagramFramingTests.cs` — round-trip 1-byte header mọi loại + DATA payload + reject empty datagram; `OpenConnectConnectCodecTests.cs` — parse X-DTLS-Session-ID/CipherSuite/Port/DPD/Keepalive + `HasDtls` + advertise DTLS trong CONNECT request). Test live SSTP/L2TP (~12) vẫn gắn `[Trait("Category","Integration")]`. **Runner = xUnit v3** (mỗi project test là executable Microsoft.Testing.Platform, `OutputType=Exe`; cấu hình chung ở [`tests/Directory.Build.props`](../tests/Directory.Build.props)) — chạy offline mỗi project bằng `dotnet exec <Tests>.dll -trait- "Category=Integration"` (trên host bình thường `dotnet test --filter "Category!=Integration"` cũng được). Lý do đổi từ xUnit v2/VSTest: VSTest không resolve được dotnet host trên môi trường dev **Termux/PRoot arm64** ("Could not find 'dotnet' host for the 'ARM64' architecture" — process chạy dưới PRoot là `libproot-loader.so` chứ không phải muxer `dotnet`); xUnit v3 chạy thẳng assembly nên bỏ qua bước probe đó.
- ✅ **CI**: [`.github/workflows/ci.yml`](../.github/workflows/ci.yml) (GitHub Actions, ubuntu-latest, .NET 8 SDK) trên push/PR `master`/`dev` — `dotnet build` cả 2 TFM rồi chạy từng test executable offline (`-trait- "Category=Integration"`). Đa-OS (Windows/macOS) + job integration lab còn để lại (Q.5).
- ℹ️ **Ràng buộc build C# 12**: code giữ trong phạm vi C# 12 (vd ICMP echo encode tách ra method **non-async** [`TcpIpStack.BuildEchoRequest`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.IpStack/TcpIpStack.cs) để `ReadOnlySpan<byte>` local hợp lệ — "ref struct trong async" là C# 13). Nhờ vậy build xanh kể cả SDK .NET 8 (LangVersion `latest` = C# 12); không khoá lên SDK .NET 9/10.

## Khác biệt so với design docs

Các file `00`–`09` mô tả **ý định thiết kế**; vài điểm đã lệch khỏi code hiện hành:

| Design doc nói | Code thực tế |
|---|---|
| `04`: L2TP/IPsec dùng **IKEv2** | L2TP/IPsec dùng **IKEv1** ([IkeV1Client.cs:18](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Ike/V1/IkeV1Client.cs#L18)); IKEv2 nay là driver **riêng** [`Drivers.Ikev2`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Ikev2) (V.1, ESP tunnel mode không L2TP) chứ không phải transport cho L2TP |
| `00`: decorator **`EspIkeDemuxTransport`** | Không tồn tại; demux IKE/ESP nằm trong [NatTraversalChannel](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat/NatTraversalChannel.cs#L13) + vòng lặp nhận |
| `00`/`02`: tầng TRANSPORT riêng — project `Transport.Udp` là "khối dùng chung ESP-in-UDP" | Project `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Transport.Udp` đã **gom vào `Ipsec` dưới [`Nat/`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec/Nat)** (namespace `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ipsec.Nat`) — nội dung 100% đặc thù IPsec NAT-T (RFC 3947/3948), không implement `IDatagramTransport`; vai trò "khối dùng chung cho mọi ESP-over-UDP" giữ nguyên (mọi consumer đều ref `Ipsec`). Họ `Transport.Tls`/`Transport.Dtls`/`Transport.RawIp` tương lai không bị ảnh hưởng |
| `00`/`04`: tên `IVpnTransport`, `VpnConnection`, `VpnSession`, tham số `options` | Thực tế: `IVpnConnection`/`IVpnSession`, `ConnectAsync` không có `options`; transport tách `IByteStreamTransport`/`IDatagramTransport` |
| `00`: `EthernetAdapter`, `VirtualHost`, L2 multi-host | **Nền L2 đầy đủ (phase L2.0–L2.9) đã có**: project [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet) — codec `EthernetFrame`/`MacAddress` (L2.0) + [`EthernetSwitch`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetSwitch.cs#L16) học MAC (L2.1) + [`VirtualHost`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/VirtualHost.cs#L23) cầu nối L2↔L3 (L2.2) + [`ArpResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/ArpResolver.cs#L26) ARP IPv4 (L2.3) + [`NdiscResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/NdiscResolver.cs#L31) NDISC IPv6 (L2.4) + [`DhcpV4Configurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DhcpV4Configurator.cs#L30) DHCPv4 (L2.5) + [`Ipv6AddressConfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/Ipv6AddressConfigurator.cs#L34) SLAAC+DHCPv6 (L2.6) + [`EthernetAdapter`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/EthernetAdapter.cs#L24) ráp multi-host (L2.7) + [`MultiHostSession`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/MultiHostSession.cs#L25) N station = N `IVpnSession` (L2.8) + composite dual-stack [`DualStackNeighborResolver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DualStackNeighborResolver.cs#L24)/[`DualStackAddressConfigurator`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Ethernet/DualStackAddressConfigurator.cs#L22) (L2.9). Hợp đồng L2 [IEthernetChannel](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Abstractions/Channels/Interfaces/IEthernetChannel.cs#L7) **có impl src thật** (`EthernetSwitch.Port`), `VirtualHost` hiện thực **quy tắc vàng** (stack chỉ bind `IPacketChannel`), và **cả** `INeighborResolver` (ARP+NDISC, composite dual-stack) lẫn `IAddressConfigurator` (DHCPv4 + SLAAC/DHCPv6, composite dual-stack) **đều có hiện thực thật**. **Chưa**: driver L2 đa-host **data-plane** (gắn uplink VPN thật vào `EthernetAdapter` như một port); đường live mặc định vẫn thuần L3 (`IPacketChannel`). |
| `00`: data plane qua `ISecuritySession` / `IPacketEncapsulator` | 2 hợp đồng này đã **xóa ở P0.1** — shape thực tế phân kỳ (`EspSession` dùng `TryUnprotect` bool + rekey/sequence-exposure; framing thật là HDLC event-driven / `L2tpCodec` / SSTP 4-byte header). Sẽ **tái thiết kế từ ≥2 consumer thật** ở roadmap F.2. Ngược lại `IByteStreamTransport` nay **có impl** [`TlsByteStream`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp/Transport/TlsByteStream.cs#L23) (SSTP, P0.1). |
| `00`–`04`: **không** đề cập keepalive / rekey / teardown / reconnect | **Đã bổ sung as-built** cho **cả 2 driver**: L2TP/IPsec (IKE DPD + L2TP HELLO, Phase 2 rekey make-before-break, teardown CDN/StopCCN + IKE Delete — §6.1) **và** SSTP (active Echo keepalive, teardown Call-Disconnect, auto-reconnect — §7.1); cả hai dùng auto-reconnect backoff sau `SwappablePacketChannel`. SSTP không rekey (TLS sống dài). |
| OpenConnect `X-CSTP-Rekey-Method: ssl` ⇒ **renegotiate TLS** trên cùng kết nối | `SslStream` BCL trên **net8/netstandard2.0 không lộ TLS-renegotiation phía client** (`ExportKeyingMaterial`/renegotiate chỉ net9+), và driver chỉ thấy `IByteStreamTransport` (không truy cập `SslStream`) ⇒ **cả `ssl` lẫn `new-tunnel` đều xử lý bằng re-establish make-before-break** (`OpenConnectConnection.RekeyAsync`, V5.d) — IP stack không re-bind, tunnel không rớt. Renegotiate thật chờ TLS handshake riêng (BouncyCastle) hoặc target net9+. |
| `00`/`04`: 1 project driver `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers` (subfolder `L2tpIpsec/`+`Sstp/`) | Đã **tách thành 2 project** `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.L2tpIpsec` + `TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.Sstp` (file phẳng ở gốc, giữ `Enums/`+`Models/`); namespace giữ nguyên. SSTP nay **chỉ ref Abstractions + Ppp** (không còn kéo Ipsec/L2tp). |
| `01`: ràng buộc **no-admin** (userspace thuần, không cần quyền) | Đổi thành **no-admin → no-install**: admin/raw-socket nay là **tùy chọn hạng nhất** khi consumer cần proto tùy ý — **PPTP GRE (proto-47, V.6)** và **native ESP proto-50 (P0.8c)** không có đường userspace nào khác ⇒ cần `Transport.RawIp` (F.9, elevate). PPTP **V6.a (control + CCP/MPPE offline) không cần admin**; chỉ **data plane GRE runtime** (V.6 sau) mới cần. SSTP/L2TP/IKEv2/OpenVPN/WireGuard/SoftEther/OpenConnect vẫn no-admin. |
| `04`: IKEv2/PSK + transform cố định, **"Bỏ rekey/MOBIKE/EAP"** | L2TP/IPsec dùng **IKEv1** (đã nêu hàng trên); ngoài ra **đã có rekey** Phase 1 in-place ([`RekeyPhase1Async`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.L2tpIpsec/L2tpIpsecConnection.cs#L638)) + Phase 2 make-before-break + DPD + teardown — không còn "bỏ rekey". MOBIKE/cert vẫn ngoài phạm vi L2TP (cert/EAP có ở driver IKEv2 riêng). |
| `09`: TCP **"bản tối giản: no SACK, no window-scaling, cwnd nhỏ cố định"**; **"IPv6 sau"** | Stack TCP **vượt** tối giản: có **SACK** (RFC 2018), **window-scaling** (RFC 7323), **NewReno** congestion control, **PMTUD động**, half-close FSM, zero-window persist (xem README IpStack + §5/§8). **IPv6/ICMPv6 dual-stack đã làm** (header/extension-header/Fragment reassembly/ICMPv6 echo+error/Packet-Too-Big), không "để sau". |
| `08`: cô lập sau project `Crypto.Abstractions`; cột "DLL" `Crypto.Aead`/`Crypto.Mppe`/`Crypto.Noise` (DLL tách) | Tất cả trong **một project** [`TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Crypto) — `Crypto.Aead`/`Crypto.Mppe`/`Crypto.Noise` là **sub-namespace**, interface để ở `Crypto/Interfaces` (không có project `Crypto.Abstractions`). |
| `08`: "cô lập code net8-only sau `#if NET8_0_OR_GREATER`"; BouncyCastle chỉ ns2.0 | `#if` rào theo phiên bản .NET **thấp nhất** hỗ trợ API (vd `AesGcm`/`ChaCha20Poly1305` BCL từ **net5+**, không khoá net8); **BouncyCastle.Cryptography ref không điều kiện** cả 2 TFM (net8 cũng thiếu X25519/BLAKE2s). `record`/`init`/`required` dùng được cả 2 TFM nhờ package source-only `TqkLibrary.CompilerServices`. |
| `02`: bảng "Khối dùng chung (DLL)" — `Transport.Udp`/`Transport.Tls`/`Crypto.Noise`/`Crypto.Mppe` là DLL riêng | `Transport.Udp` **đã gom vào `Ipsec`** (`…Ipsec.Nat`); `Transport.Tls` hiện vẫn là `TlsByteStream` **trong driver SSTP** (F.1 sẽ nâng ra chung); `Crypto.Noise`/`Crypto.Mppe` là **sub-namespace** trong project `Crypto`; `Transport.Dtls` **đã tách project**; `Transport.RawIp` **đã build** (F.9 — `RawIpDatagramTransport`/`RawIpTransportFactory`, consumer đầu tiên P0.8c native ESP). |
| `01`: ràng buộc **no-admin** (client thuần userspace, không cần quyền nâng cao) | **Đã nới: no-admin → no-install.** Mặc định vẫn no-admin; raw socket/elevate là **tùy chọn hạng nhất** chỉ khi consumer cần — hiện là **P0.8c native ESP proto-50** (gateway IP-public không-NAT), opt-in qua `IRawIpTransportFactory` (null = no-admin như cũ). Windows **best-effort** (OS IPsec/IKEEXT hoặc firewall có thể nuốt proto-50 inbound); Linux `CAP_NET_RAW` là môi trường tham chiếu. F.9 cũng mở đường cho V6.b PPTP-GRE (proto-47) + V.8 IP-in-IP. |
| `07`: watermark SoftEther "**server chỉ cần đúng dòng POST**" (blob placeholder là đủ) | **SAI với server thật**: SoftEther server chính chủ (VPN Gate) trả **HTTP 403** cho watermark placeholder ⇒ cần **watermark blob THẬT** (dữ liệu GPL — KHÔNG commit; nạp runtime từ file qua tham số `watermark` của [`SoftEtherDriver`](../src/TqkLibrary.VpnClient.Drivers.SoftEther/SoftEtherDriver.cs#L49) / demo `--watermark`). Test offline (server giả lập) vẫn chấp nhận placeholder. |

---
*Tạo bằng cách đọc song song toàn bộ subsystem + truy vết 2 luồng connect, đối chiếu trực tiếp mã nguồn.*
